Mais en cestui ovraige est paour ou li malaides muert maintenant, ou fistule i vient qui ne puet estre sanee.	But in this work, there is fear of the patient dying now, or a fistula may come which cannot be healed.
de la mice	of the mouse
Quant tu cures la maladie de la mice de ceu que nos avons dit as divisions des cures, et il ne profite mie, adonques i afierent III manieres de cautere que tuit sont boin.	When you treat the disease of the mouse as we have said in the divisions of treatments, and it does not improve, then they recommended three methods of cauterization that are all good.
Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant;	In one manner, you should make three cauterizations, or four, in a line along the length of the thigh, according to the shape of the liver cautery that we mentioned earlier;
et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos;	and do not press your hand on the entire cauterization area, and have the patient lie on their back;
et une autre maniere de cautere si est que tu eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners, si com nos l’avons mostreit en la dislocation de l’espaule;	and another method of cauterization is to heat the double-sided cautery as we have shown in the case of shoulder dislocation;
et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	and lift the leg that is on the affected side, where the wound of the patient comes from the left, and let the elevations you use to lift the leg be according to the length of the limb, and the cauterizations be according to the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII.	After inserting the two inflamed nerves until the pain is felt on the other side, then draw out the cautery, and thus there will be four.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	And if you wish, cauterize the entire cautery with three nerves.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After the treatment when it has expelled pus for a long time, and this is worth more than the others of the previously mentioned treatments.
de ydropisie	of hydropsy
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Cautery is not effective for a person with hydropsy, except in the manner called "asclytes".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis;	When you treat it according to the methods we have described in divisions, and your treatment does not help, then you must make four cauteries around the buttocks, one on the stomach, one on the liver, one near the armpit, two behind the back on the spine, and one near the hip.
et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	and let the cauteries be close to the place of the pain.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere;	After leaving the cautery open to expel pus for a long time, do not leave the treatment of the patient after the cautery;
et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	and healing should be expedited, and both intentions will be together with the help of God.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit;	The form of the cautery for the abdomen should be the clamp that we have shown before;
et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	and the one for the back should be olive-shaped, as it is placed above here;
de l’enfleure des piez	of foot swelling
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire;	When the feet are swollen in one who is suffering from dropsy and are filled with yellow fluid, you must cauterize on the back of the foot between the little finger and the ring finger;
et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	and lift your hand with the cautery as you turn.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too deeply, lest you hit the heart, and let the cauterization be in this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire;	After make two cauterizations on each leg at the tip of the kneecap;
et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe;	and let the cauterizations be long, one above the knee in front and the other below the knee, in the middle of the leg;
et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse;	and leave the cauterizations uncovered for a long time without cleaning, so the pus can drain;
aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	after performing the other treatments that we have mentioned.
de la menoison	of massage
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;	When a resolution of the abdomen comes from cold and moisture, such that the retentive and digestive virtues in the stomach and intestines are weakened, and cannot be cured by usual methods;
et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;	And you see the patient suffering greatly and of great strength, so make a large cautery on the stomach as has been described above in the section about the cautery of the stomach, to the circular cautery;
et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	And four small cauteries around the mouth, and one small cross-shaped cautery, and two cauteries on the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see the moisture abundant and the patient suffering, make a cautery on the wrist, and one cautery on each nodule, and two small cauteries on the stomach near the large one, for the treatment is beneficial when there is good assistance.
de la cure des emorroydes	on the treatment of hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres:	When hemorrhoids are in the fundament, one or more, and they are old and consist of cold and moist corrupted humors, and have been treated as we said in the divisions, and it does not help, then make cauteries:
III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois;	Three on the spine of the back, those that are farthest out from the hip bone and bone in a triangular pattern, and two below the mouth, one should be made;
et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile;	And if you think his stomach is chilled, and the meat does not cook, and one sees swelling on the face, then place a large cautery over the stomach as was previously mentioned, and another over the liver, and yet another over the spleen for the entire cautery process.
et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	And leave the cautery in place for a long time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After treating the area until it is healthy.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the flesh condition which is called "thelul
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit;	When you apply althaea, heat the cautery that appears like a razor, and then place it fully ignited on the applied althaea.
et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort;	And keep your hand there until the cautery reaches the beginning of the vein, where the blood is cut off;
fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit;	do this once or twice, and if there is much althaea, cauterize each area as we have said;
aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez;	after the treatment of beneficial ointments until they are healed;
et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	and if you cauterize with a large cautery on the affected area, it will be more effective.
de plaie mal curee	of an improperly treated wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot endure incision or opening, which we will discuss in its place, if such an illness comes that cannot be healed except by cautery.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When fistula comes to someone and is inflamed, discharging pus and corrupt moisture, then you should immediately apply a fine tent, and be sure to know the depth of the tent at all times.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing;	Heat the cautery which resembles a razor, and insert it into the fistula according to the extent that the tent has entered, and repeat the cauterization until the diseased and corrupted flesh is burned, once or twice or three times, as needed.
et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	and be careful not to burn the nerves that are nearby and the large veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans;	if the fistula leads to the body of the bladder and to the intestines, be careful around these areas, and do not perform such procedures except in fleshy parts, and remember that it is not safe there.
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement;	After treating the wound until it is healed, and if the pus has been drained, and the matter has been removed for a long time, then you can know that the wound is completely healed;
et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font;	and if the matter has not been removed, know that the wound is still present, and the bone may become corrupted;
et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	and thus as one of those we will mention in its place.
de la maladie des reins	of the disease of the kidneys
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit;	When pain from cold comes to the thighs, and due to large flatus, and if it does not respond to female treatment, then you must perform a cautery on both sides of the thighs with the cross-shaped cautery that we mentioned earlier;
et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	and if we perform the cautery in the middle, there will be three cauteries in a line, and they will provide more assistance.
de la vessie	of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce;	When the bladder is weak and feeble from cold and moisture, so that the patient retains urine, then make a cautery on the outer part above the bladder where the hairs of the pubic region begin, one on each side, and let each cautery be as long as the width of a finger;
et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing;	and make one cautery outside the back, or two if you need them;
et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	and let the cauterizations be shaped as described above.
de la marris	of the swelling
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde;	When the womb is cold and moist, and does not allow conception for that reason, and the flowers are corrupted and their terms delayed;
et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor:	and when they come, there is great pain:
adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos;	Then it is necessary that three cauterizations be performed around the mouth, as we have said for the cauterization of the bladder, and two cauterizations on either side of the back;
et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	and let the cauterizations be made with a clamp, as we have said.
de la hainche	of the thigh
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble;	When the viscous fluids descend to the hip joint, and because of this it moves from its place, and the sign is that one thigh is longer than the other when measured together;
et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle;	and if the place of origin is found nearby, it is necessary that you cauterize the patient on the hip joint with a cautery resembling a circle, and mark in front of the area around the joint as it turns, so that the joint lies within the circle;
et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	And let the cauterizations be such as those used to cauterize the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs;	And if these cauterizations are not present, make three large olive oil cauterizations, and let the cauterizations be as deep as all other burns;
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat it until it is healed.
de la dolor de la hainche	of the pain in the thigh
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene:	When pain comes in the thigh joint, and it is due to coldness and moisture, and the patient is treated with what we have mentioned in the division, but the treatment does not help, and the illness is old:
adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	then it is necessary that you purge the patient of thick humors with foul-smelling pills or other similar good pills.
Aprés li fai cautere;	After performing cauterization;
et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres:	and the method of cauterization is according to two methods:
c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	that is to say, together with burning medicines, and fire cauterization.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz:	Fire cauterization is according to many methods, of which one is such:
que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire;	that you cauterize on the buttock of the thigh three triangular cauterizations according to this form, and make them deep and large, and have between each cautere a space the thickness of one finger, and let the cauterizations be olive-shaped;
aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	Sometimes a cauterization is made in the middle on top of the thigh head, for which there are four according to this form:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche;	And if you wish, cauterize with the circular cautery that we mentioned earlier in the hip dislocation;
mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	but do it in such a way that the circle covers the entire hip, and all the nerves be cauterized.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the way it is done for sciatica, when the pain is in the hip and does not reach as far as the thigh or the leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc;	And if it reaches the thigh and leg, make two cauterizations where the patient says the pain is, and one cauterization above the ankle four digits to the left side;
et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur;	and let the cauterizations be shallow, and burn only the thickness of the nerve;
et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	and if the patient feels that the pain extends to two digits of the foot or nearby, cauterize where they feel the pain three points or four with the cautery called "points.
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus;	And if necessary, do more of it;
et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if he knows that the pain is below the knee towards the thigh, do a cautery with the cutellaire or circular cautery, and take great care in all your cauterizations that you do not leave it so long that you burn the nerves and large arteries, and that you do not cause the patient greater harm and contraction.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I myself have seen many who applied a cauterization on the ankle of the foot, and they left it burning so much that the entire leg became swollen, and the foot as well, and it was pierced and the whole foot corrupted.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a belly treatment from which he died.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is in two parts at once, apply cauterization to both, according to this method.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce;	And the wise ones said about the cautery of the thigh, of which here is the manner, make it such that it is at the head as thick as a date seed, or a little less, and let it be between the joints, and from one joint to the other let there be a space of a barleycorn in length;
et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait;	and let the crosspieces be on both sides, and let them also be like bolts, and there should be one iron handle well made;
et c’est li forme:	and this is the form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit;	And heat it until it is completely red and sparks fly, and then place it upon the side of the diseased thigh, and turn it towards the healthy side;
et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors;	and let the patient undergo one cautery session and leave it for three days;
et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens;	and then make a plaster of butter, and leave the wound open for a long time;
aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	after treating it with ointment until it is healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent;	Albucasis says that we use this cautery little due to fear of his regard, and if we see few who use it;
et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	and still this is one of the good cauteries, which can be tolerated by those who suffer from it.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi;	The cautery of burning medicine is such that you make the instrument with interstices in which descends the margin of the door, and it should be of brass or iron along one side, and at its height have two notches, and between each have the thickness of a finger.
et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	and let them be open at both ends and join together according to this form:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche;	After place the box of the thigh on the patient lying on their healthy side, and then place your hand much upon the box of the thigh;
aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After pour it between the two circles of hot water that has been heated over the fire for one hour, and let the patient experience the warmth and burning sensation.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;	For it causes a bite as from fire;
et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;	and when the burning sensation has passed, lift your hand with the instrument and raise the hip in warm water, and leave it this way for three days, and apply butter until the blackness from the scald is removed;
et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;	and let him rest for three days so that pus may be discharged;
et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	and this would be the final aid after the treatment of poultices until he is healed.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;	And if the pain has spread to the thigh or to the leg, make the instrument that fits according to what you have done for the thigh similarly;
et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	and this is the method for making it hot, and I have written it in the treatise on the preparation of medicines.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take alkaline substances and quicklime, an equal amount of each, and grind them together, then put them in a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;	where there is a small opening that allows the tip of a razor to enter;
et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;	and place another pot over that one, which is well leaded, and put alkaline substances and charcoal on it, with a layer of powder above, until there are two layers of powder above the prepared powders;
et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	and leave it like this until water and pieces come out of the leaded pot, then take all that liquid and pour it over charcoal and alkaline substances as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.	And then it will be very severe and is treated with various medical practices and cauterizations of other limbs.
Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	For it performs work like fire, and there are other medicines with which one can cauterize the thigh well as in the case of decoctions made from honey and anacardium and salt mixed together with soap.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Galien tells us of a cure where a man was treated for pain in the hip and sciatic nerve, and he praises it highly, and says that no other treatment was done, and he was healed in one session when this cure was performed, and he bathed as he teaches hereafter.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie;	And he says in this manner that you should take green fresh litharge and dry it, and grind it much with a little grease, and apply it to the thigh, leg, or shin where the pain lies, and bind it.
et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	and leave it on for three hours until the patient no longer feels the burning sensation.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then have him enter the bath until his body is slightly refreshed, and then put him to bed, and the pain will completely go away and he will be healed.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And know that no one must use such medicinal cauterization unless it is after the evacuation of pus.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout;	And Dioscorides says that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with goat hair, it helps greatly;
et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	and the cauterization should be performed in such a manner.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take wool and grease it with old oil, and place it on the hollow that is between the big toe of the foot and the one called fuscule.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	After taking dry goat hair, hold it over fire until it turns to charcoal, and place it on the wool, leaving it there until it is extinguished;
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	and do it again in the same way, and continue doing so until you believe by sense that it reaches up to the thigh, and the pain is ceased;
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	and this method of cauterization is called "goat hair cauterization".
de la dolor dou dos	of the pain in the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether from falling or impact or from excessive bloodletting, or from substances spread out cold, none of these cases is suitable for cauterization except for that which comes from an influx of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	It is necessary after the patient has been voided of stinking pills or other similar substances, that three lines be marked on the back where the pain resides, and in each line five cauteries or more according to the virtue and quantity that the patient can endure;
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	and let the cauterizations be done according to the cautery which is called "points";
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	and if you wish, make three or four cauterizations at the middle clavicle according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	This illness often comes to small children, and the signs of its beginning are that they have difficulty raising their arms and are afraid;
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	And you find in the last spine of the back and in its appearance which comes above the other spines.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and you wish to treat it, cauterize it with the ball cautery according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	So that the cautery affects each part of the spine equally.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you wish, cauterize around the spine with the pointed cautery in two or three lines, and let the points be close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After treating the area until it is healed as we have said, and be careful not to apply a cautery to a swelling that is in a nerve cramp.
de la dolor des jointes	of the pain of the joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	When joint pain is caused by moisture that spreads to each member of the body, and when pain comes in the feet, which physicians call "podagra" properly, and when it is due to a cold cause and medicines cannot cure it, then it is treated with cautery in such a manner:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	Make the moles of cauterization around the joint of the foot, and let the cauterizations be olive-shaped according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if there is need to cauterize the sole of the foot, then make the cauterization as one calls it "point" across the entire area.
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	And if the pains come up to the knees and other joints, which happens many times, make cauterizations on each knee III cauterizations or IIII of each part, making all the cauterizations olive-shaped;
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you need more, do more, but hold back your hand except until the scar on the heart is burned.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend to the knees and back, then administer the cautery that we have mentioned in its chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	And if the pains are in the hands, make poultices around the wrist for two lines;
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	and if any pain remains in the two hands, make poultices on each joint and on the hair of the hand;
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	and if the pains come up to the elbows or up to the shoulders, cauterize each part, and take good care of the patient with potent medicines.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you give it proper treatment and purge phlegm, then with God’s help he will be well.
de la routure dou syfac	of the fracture of the cheekbone
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	When rupture comes in groins, and the balls descend to the thighs and this is newly happened, then it must be that when you wish to treat him, he must eat nothing that day;
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	and that he uses things that loosen the belly so that the feces come out of his belly;
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	after you make him sit on his back between your hands, and instruct him to hold his breath until the eye is repositioned, and reset them with your two fingers, and cut from behind the rupture over the bone of the thumb, and make one sign that resembles half a circle above the body;
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	then heat the cautery which has this shape:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	until they are white and shed scales.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	Then reset the eyes to their place;
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	and the minister hold his hand so that they do not move back;
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	And work well on the patient’s thighs, and place under him one cushion and one towel on the thighs, and another under the buttocks to hold the hands.
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	Then place the cautery on the mark with your entire hand, and hold it straight until you reach the bone, and if you do not reach it the first time, repeat it again until you reach the bone.
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	And be careful that the flesh does not come out when you perform the cautery;
que tu ne le brulasses;	that you do not burn it;
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	and that the patient does not die because of it, or suffer another harm.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And know that when you do not reach the bone with the cautery, your work is worth nothing.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	And it is necessary that the cauterizations for children be delicate according to their measure, and for adults also large according to their measure;
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	after three days, treat the area of the butter cauterization until the burn is gone;
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	after that, treat with other ointments until he is healed, and have the patient lie on his back for forty days until the wound is well sealed;
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	and it is necessary that his nursing be prolonged so that the eyes do not protrude when he tries to go into chambers.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	And after forty days, when he wishes to rise, provide him with a well-made bandage, and have him wear it for another forty days;
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	and let him have good rest, that he work little and guard against excessive overeating and drinking, and too much loud talking;
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	and when he follows this teaching, he is completely healed.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will say hereafter the treatment for cutting in his chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	of the rupture of the abdomen
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	When ruptures occur in other parts of the body and are known, and you wish that they do not grow larger, apply the cautery according to their size, and let a third part be burned.
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	after the treatment as we have said;
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	and some of the ancients have said that it should be cauterized at three points according to this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	but mark the site first and draw a line across the width above the rupture, and another below, and proceed step by step throughout the entire cautery.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first cauterizations are lighter and gentler.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of old pain in any limb
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain comes to any limb, whether from falling or being injured, and that pain lasts long, and medical treatment is of no use, then it must be cauterized with the cautery called "points," and the cauterization should follow the length of the limb and its smallness and weakness and strength and location of twists and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	if he is well from the first cauterization, it is good;
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If that happens, restart the other cautery on top of it, because such is custom that they must change to the nearest limb, so you must perform the cauteries until the patient is healed.
de meselerie	of mixing/misuse/malpractice
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	The ailments are sometimes cured by cautery with great assistance, and especially those diseases that come from the putrefaction of phlegm and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	When you see that it needs to be cauterized, take care if the patient is in the beginning stages, and if it is treated as we have described in the division, and neither desists nor delays, and you fear that corruption will spread throughout the patient, then perform V cauteries on the head:
I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;	Place one nine inches from the top of the head, and the other towards the forehead at the end of the hair;
et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;	and two above the two temples, and one behind on the occipital region;
et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;	and leave your hand there until the cauterization reaches the bone, and until the bark comes out so that the vapors of thick humors can escape;
et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	and cauterize on the mouse according to what is in front of it.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;	And if the disorder is scattered everywhere;
et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;	and if it is clearly manifested, then you must cauterize with the cauterizations that we have mentioned at the head, and one cauterization in the neck, and two cauterizations on the nape of the neck, and six cauterizations along the spine, and one large one on the buttocks and another nearby, and two on the shoulders;
et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;	and two on the ribs, and two on the heels, and one on each joint of the hands and feet, and on the hollows of the hands;
et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;	and beware of the nerves that are on top of the heel bone so you do not burn them;
et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	and sometimes a cautery is performed on the bone of the little finger, and another on the bone of the breastbone, and another on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;	And know that the more cauteries you perform, the more help you give, and it benefits the patient;
et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	and know that the patient does not feel pain from the cautery as a healthy person would, because the body is already completely corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	And it is necessary that the cauterizations be large and small according to the limbs and joints, according to what you find in the ways of iron.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After treatment, apply flour of wheat with honey to the area and other treatments until it is healed.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;	When swelling occurs in any limb and is treated with medicines, oils, and plasters, but it does not heal, then you should perform cauterizations on the limb according to its size;
et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;	And let the cauterization penetrate a little into the thickness of the heart;
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it with ointments until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;	And sometimes cauterization is done to the hand and foot and back, at the nerve that controls the limb, and thus the swelling is removed;
et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	and in any case, do not involve anyone who is not knowledgeable about the limbs and the nerves that move the body.
de albaras	of alum
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;	When the illness called "albaras" is severe, and medicinal remedies are ineffective, then cauterize it with a cautery slightly deep, according to the thickness of the heart, until the pallor is removed, and its color changes.
puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie;	Then treat with flour of barley and lentils with rose oil and plantain leaves, and sparrow blood and lark blood, of each an equal part;
et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	and mix it all together, and wrap it in a cloth, and apply it to the place until it is healed.
li cure de chancre par cautere	the treatment of a sore using cauterization
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When a sore appears at the beginning and you wish to stop its progress, cauterize it with a cautery that forms a circle around the entire perimeter of the sore.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre;	And always the wise said that one should perform cauterization in the middle of the ulcer;
et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;	and always I do not think this is good, for I fear that it may ulcerate and corrupt, and I have seen it happen some times;
et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	and a more proper thing is to cauterize around it, with the cautery called "circulus," as we have said regarding many types of cauterizations.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	of the swelling that cannot be cured
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens;	When someone has a disease called "adubelati," and it delays death either because of the excess it produces or because of the age of the patient when they are decrepit (that is, too old) and there is little blood, or because of the season;
et tu la vues haster de meurer:	and you see it hastening death:
adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant;	then cauterize it with many small cauteries by pricking;
aprés le laisse ensi.	after leaving it like this.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For she will hasten to kill.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you wish to pierce it completely with the cautery, then heat the cautery as follows:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And place your hand in the middle of the disease called "adubelati" until the cautery has pierced the heart, and make the cautery such that the patient feels it from outside in such a way that the course of the putrefaction is alleviated.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the treatment until it is completely healed.
li cure dou feu par fer	the fire cautery with iron
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	There is another type of disease called "corrodens," and it is nothing other than a member consumption, for it consumes the limbs just as fire consumes dry wood.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;	If you see this disease in a place that can withstand cauterization with fire together, then heat the cauteries very small and large, according to what is appropriate for the location where the disease is;
aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	After the cautery on all sides until you reach all the corruption, and there remains nothing of it, so that everything that is corrupted be removed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	Then leave it for three days, and place the affected areas that have been cauterized to soak in oil until the burns from the fire are removed, and all the corruption is gone.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the treatment with ointments that generate flesh.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin;	And if after three days you see no healthy tissue grow, that is good;
et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	and if it does not, then restart the cautery on what remains unhealed from the corrupted area.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu;	And this treatment has sometimes been cured with medication instead of the fire cautery;
mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:	but the fire cautery is of greater help, and I have already described the treatment with the medicinal agent in the section:
pren la quant tu en as mestier.	take it when you need it.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	pains that come to the feet
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Many times a disease arises in the feet from outside which is called "clos" according to our understanding, and it is a swollen thing that hinders the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the cauterizations for this disease are according to two methods.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	That is to say, fire cauterization, and hot water cauterization.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	Fire cautery is such that you heat it until it is as hot as a feather of an eagle, and it should be made of good iron to the measure that it can penetrate like a nail from all sides, and there should be fine edges;
aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;	after placing it completely on the nail, and turn your hand all around the nail until it reaches the bottom of the nail;
et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;	and leave it like this for three days until it begins to discharge pus;
puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	then apply a poultice of wild mallows crushed with salt, and leave the poultice on all night, and the nail will fall out and be uprooted from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the wound with an ointment that promotes flesh growth until it is healed.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;	And if they are turned outward from the body, and this often happens in hands and feet, then you must apply a hot water cautery to them;
et est en teil maniere:	and it is done in the following manner:
pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;	take a chain of iron or steel, or a feather of vaultul, and place it over the nail and althea leaves, which are used to remove warts;
et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;	and place the chain so that it surrounds completely, then pour some hot water on it, and hold firmly with your hand, pressing your hand around so that the edge of the chain comes to the base of the nail, and thus allow the hot water to penetrate deeply to the root;
et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;	and allow the patient to suffer a little from the bite of the hot water for an hour;
puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	then leave it like that, and it will completely uproot itself along with all its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	Do one after another until you have treated all those that are on the body, then treat them with ointments that generate flesh.
li cure dou trembler	the treatment for trembling
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;	When someone shivers from cold sweat due to nerves, or from a fever of four days, or otherwise, you must perform IV cauterizations on the spine, one cauterization between each vertebra.
et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire;	and one cauterization on the foot, and one above the stomach at the olive cauterization;
si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	this will stop the shivering and hasten the recovery from the cold illness.
des pustules puans	the treatment for foul pus-filled sores
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	At times, baths or foul pus-filled sores appear on the surface of the body, which come from large corrupted matters.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule:	It is necessary at first, when they appear, to make a cauterization on each head of the pustule:
un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	a delicate cautery made from the branch of myrtle, whose tip is heated by fire, or from a long root of arisotle (celandine), or a lentil-shaped cautery.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez;	And sometimes they are cauterized at the beginning when they appear, in this manner, and they cannot grow anymore from then on, but the excess that causes them is broken up, and they are healed;
mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	but it must be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	when the artery is cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses;	Many times there are great hemorrhages from the artery that is cut at the wound coming from the side, or from incising an abscess, or from cauterizing a limb, and similar things;
et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	And it is a very grave thing to extinguish.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus;	And whenever this happens to anyone, hurry to place your finger on the wound of the vein, and press very hard until the blood is stilled beneath your finger, and no more oozes out;
puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge;	then place the olive cauterizes in the fire, several small and large ones until they are all red;
puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	then take one, either large or small according to the wound and where the artery is exposed, and place the cauterize on that vein where you are pressing with your finger, and hold it there until the blood is stilled.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if it spurts out when you lift your thumb from the vein, and the cauterizers have gone out, quickly take another of the cauterizers that are in the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez;	And do not stop doing this one after another until the bleeding is stopped;
et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide;	and beware that you do not burn the nerve which is nearby, and that no other harm comes to the patient;
et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit:	and note that when the vein becomes detached from the artery, one cannot properly reattach it oneself when the artery is large, unless it is done by one of the four methods we have mentioned:
ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	by cautery, or by extraction when it is not treated, or by tightly binding with thread, or by applying medicines that have the power to reunite blood;
et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	and let it be tied and compressed appropriately.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Who will administer a foul smell by tightly wrapping cloths or placing burning things on them, or other similar things, if it does no good even if possible.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne;	And if this happens to someone and there is no physician or medicine present, then he should place his thumb on the wound of the vein as we have said, and stretch it well until it is reattached over the wound and over the vein;
et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez;	and do not move it, but moisten it with very cold water often until the blood is chilled and thickened and stinks.
et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	and apply what is needed of cauterizations and medications to him.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	Here begins the second book of treatments for wounds
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres;	We have told you in the first chapter about every disease in which a fire cauterization or hot medication is necessary, and we explained the reasons, causes, instruments, and forms of the cauterizations;
et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	and I have placed that chapter from the head to the feet, and in this chapter, I will follow the same order so that what one wishes to find can be discovered more easily.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And so as I begin this, it is necessary, dear friend, that you learn that in this chapter there is greater risk and fear of the cauteries than in the first one, and therefore greater caution is required.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses;	For in the work of this chapter, there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things;
ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I warn you that you do not undertake folly.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For many kinds of people come for treatment.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice;	such are those who become so enraged by their illness that they change slightly due to the frenzy caused by their disease, and because of the severity of their suffering;
et de ces doit on avoir paor.	and one must fear these.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit:	And there are those among them who give their senses and say:
«atendez, je sui garis»;	wait, I am cured";
et li maladie est despitouse.	and the illness is despised.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los;	It is not right for you to consent to those who come to you with this manner, but place greater honor in your dignity than in your desire, and do not act foolishly but wisely concerning what you are certain of, and from which you can gain respect and praise.
et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie;	and use prognosis and indications in the treatment of your patients where health may be restored;
et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	and this will help you achieve a good reputation, and glory, and praise-worthy memory.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Most dear child, Our Lord grant you good understanding and uprightness, and if you wish to breathe in the holy inspiration of his hand, amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	Now I have ordered this chapter by dividing it into sections, as it is before the chapter on cauterizations, which I have described from head to foot, so that you may find more easily what you will need.
dou chief plein d’aigue	the head full of fluid
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant;	Know that this illness often comes to children at birth, and when the head of the child is held too tightly;
et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	and sometimes it comes for reasons that are unknown.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors;	And I have never seen this illness except in children, and in all those whom I have seen it hastened death;
et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	and for this reason it seems to me that I should leave such treatments.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir;	And I saw a child whose head was full of water, and the head swelled each day until he could not sustain it;
et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os;	and the moisture increased so much that he died, and this moisture is gathered under the bone above the phlegm, between the heart and the bone;
et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large;	and the procedure is such that if the moisture is between the heart and the bone, and the abscess is small, you should cut a wide incision in the head;
et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre;	and it should be as long as two fingers, until the moisture flows;
et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	and see here the form of the spatula:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai II fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the swelling is larger, and the abscesses are bigger, make two cuts in the shape of a cross, according to this form:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut:	And if the moisture is out of the bone, and you see the seams of the head open on each part, and the fluid jumps outward when you press it with your hand from within, and this does not respond to you:
si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	it is necessary for you to cut three incisions in the head according to this manner:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision, remove all the moisture outside.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor;	After cleaning the incisions with cloths and powders, and putting wine and oil on them, leave it like this until the fifth day;
puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	then loosen it, and treat the wound with bandages and ointments, and clean the head evenly, and give the patient dried meat to eat with little moisture until the limb is healed and healthy.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue;	And another way of incising is to look at where the abscess is clearly swollen, and the gathering of the fluid;
car aucune fois est elle devant;	for sometimes it is in front;
aucune fois derrier;	sometimes behind;
aucune fois en destre;	sometimes on the right;
et aucune fois en senestre.	and sometimes on the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir;	Cut then there where the abscess is clearly visible, and the accumulation of fluid, and make the incision according to your ability;
et warde que tu ne coper l’artere;	and be careful not to cut the artery;
et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	and if blood flows, so that the patient dies from loss of blood and evacuation of moisture.
de reume	of rheumatism
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les II arteres.	When someone falls ill with a disease called "cataract" in the eyes or worse, and the illness is old, and medical treatment does no good, then the final remedy is cauterization using that which will cut the two arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief;	It is necessary, when you are to cut the veins, that the patient lie with his head back;
aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel;	after which you should rub the area with a rough cloth until the arteries become visible, then have the patient pull his neck against the entire cloth;
puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues;	then look where the vein lies, and their locations are behind the ears, and they are somewhat hidden;
puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	then mark the spots clearly, then cut both veins with a sharp scalpel from two sides, until the vein reaches the bone, and this should be done along the side of the head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com II dois au traver.	And if you wish, place the spatula beneath the artery and the cloth above, cutting as II should across.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is cut, the blood continuously spurts outward forcefully.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os;	And if the artery does not become visible to touch, you should measure a space of three fingers, then mark it clearly and cut down to the bone;
et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere;	and the amount of blood that should be let out is six unciae, and perhaps a bit more or less, according to what the patient can tolerate, and the fullness of the artery;
puis regarde la plaie:	then examine the wound:
s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	if it remains on the bone joint, cut it so that abscesses do not occur, then clean and bandage the wound, and treat it with ointment until it is healed.
de emigrainne	Of migraine
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When an old migraine comes with a sharp catarrh, due to the moisture of tears and heat in the temples and an ancient frenzied sweat and similar things, and it is treated by methods of medical care but nothing helps, then we extract the arteries of the temples and apply cautery as we have described.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit;	And the method of extracting them is that the patient should lie behind the hair on their temples, and listen to the artery that appears in the temple, for it beats clearly, and is slightly visible except in some people who are too cold;
et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement;	and if it is responded to, the patient should press their neck with some cloths, then rub the area with a rough cloth, and wash the area with hot water until the artery becomes clearly visible;
puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	then take the spatula which has this shape:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie;	then scrape the skin lightly until you reach the artery, then trace it up to the joints, and carefully separate it from the tissues on each side;
et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	and if the artery is delicate, use the tip of the hook to handle it, then cut it from that part according to the size of two fingers.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	For if it is not cut, the blood will not flow completely.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III;	And draw blood from six places, up to three;
et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc;	And if the artery is large, then you must tie it in two places with a strong double thread of silk, so that no corruption comes before the healing of the wound, and to prevent bleeding.
puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez;	Then cut away the excess that is between the two ties at that same moment, and then, if you wish, apply the fire cauterization with a cautery knife down to the bone until the ends are even.
et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	And this is the principal work, if the patient does not have a fever and has a warm constitution.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors:	For cauterization is aid to finish off moisture:
por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	for it is of greater help with moist conditions.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites;	For it is necessary for the extraction of arteries that one fill the place with old cotton and put on well-made bandages;
et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and when they are untied, one should be careful with dry medicines that promote flesh growth and bandages until it is healed;
et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez;	and if the artery is cut as much as you work on it, hurry to cauterize where you fill the place with vitriol and pull it with your hand so that the blood stops;
et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient;	and if you do not have it available, place your thumb on the spot as long as the blood stops, and rinse the area with cold water until the bleeding ceases, and bind it as is appropriate;
et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	And for those who are weaker and lighter in the extraction of the artery is that you cauterize the vein with this cutting cautery from two sides, but let the cuts be well spaced to preserve their heat longer.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	For when the instrument is too cold, it holds less of its heat.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus;	There should be a space of about one finger's width between the two knives, and then when you have marked the two places, place the hot iron on until it reaches the bone, and cut the vein in two places;
et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout;	and let them be spaced between the two joints because they are not to be joined together by this entire cautery;
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	and this is the form of the cautery:
des larmes	of tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis;	When the tears from the eyes come down from the veins that are above the forehead due to heat, and it does not benefit from any medicinal treatment you apply, and you see the patient's face turn red, and feel the forehead with a shaking motion as if trembling;
et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.
