And when the eyes are swollen and moist so that the hairs of the eyelids fall out, and the eyelids are heated and scorched by the heat of tears, then this treatment is necessary.
Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», et est que tu faices a rere au malaide qui a ceste maladie les poilz qu’il ait ou front, puis li fai III fendures ou front igalment selonc la longesce dou front;	And the ancients called it "contusion treatment," and it is that you make the patient lie down who has this illness, then shave the hair from their forehead, and make three incisions on the forehead evenly according to its length;
et soit l’une des fendures ausi com II doi tout emmi lou front en avalant aval jusc’a neif, et les autres II as II costelz par desus les papieres, et te garde de l’incision des arteres que sont as II costez par desus les papieres;	and one of the incisions should be made in the middle two fingers' width above the eyebrows and extend down to the nose, and the other two should be made on either side near the temples, and be careful not to cut into the arteries that are on both sides near the temples;
et aloigne ta main de la continuation des II mandibules, et soit chescune plaie la quantiteit de III dois au traver joins;	and move your hand away from the continuation of the two mandibles, and let each wound be the quantity of three digits across the joint;
et aies apparillie une piece d’esponge et mout de drapelz ses por essuer lou sanc, puis boute le spatumile agut de II pars de coi ci est li forme:	and prepare a piece of sponge and much cloth to wipe the blood, then place the spatula sharp from both sides as shown in this form:
des l’incision qui est dever la temple jusc’a la seconde incision;	from the incision which is near the temple to the second incision;
et escorche tout le keur qui est entre les II fendures a tot lou syfac qui est sus l’os, puis fai autreteil des la moiene incision jusc’a l’autre seconde, et puis estrai fuer cest spatumile.	and peel all the flesh which is between the two cuts to the surface that is on the bone, then do the same from the middle incision to the other second one, and then remove this spatula.
si boute en la premiere fendure l’estrument qui est apelez «cultellaire», et est tresbien trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part est souef, ne mie trenchans, et c’est li forme:	Insert into the first groove the instrument called "cultellaire," which is very well suited for cutting on one side, and smooth without cutting on the other side, and this is its shape:
Et met le costeit taillant vers la char aerse au keur, et lou costeit souef vers l’os, et lou boute tant qu’il veigne a la moiene fendure.	And place the cutting edge towards the flesh on the chest, and the smooth side towards the bone, and insert it until it reaches the middle groove.
Et cope toz les vasselz que dessendent dou chief as eulz tant que l’incision soit continue jusc’a ceu qui apert dou keur, et puis autreteil fai en la moiene fendure jusc’a l’autre defuer;	And cut all the vessels that descend from the head to the eyes so that the incision is continuous until it reaches the one that opens into the flesh, and then do the same in the middle incision until the other end.
et puis estrai dou sanc igalment, et espresse lou leu por le sanc pris;	Then draw out the blood evenly, and press the area to expel the remaining blood;
puis met en chescune fendure une tente de viel coton, et met sus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile et en aisil, et garde que apostemes chaus n’i veigne;	Then place a piece of old cotton in each wound, and cover with cloths soaked in wine, oil, and pitch, and guard against the formation of pus-filled abscesses;
et au tier jor deslie lou liien, et i amenistre grant planteit d’aigue tede, puis lou cure d’oignement basilicon avec oile roset, et d’autres cures dont on cure plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And on the third day loosen the bandage, and apply a large poultice of water parsley, then treat with basilicon ointment mixed with rose oil, and other treatments used for wounds, until he is healed.
dou reume des eulz	of the rheum of the eyes
Quant a aucun vienent catarre agut acostumeement, et tu vois les eulz tenves et petis, et afoiblir la veue, et les papieres brulees;	When someone frequently suffers from acute catarrh, and you see the eyes swollen and small, with weakened vision, and the eyelids reddened;
et li poil chieent, et ou chief en parfont a dolor ague, et li malaides esternue;	and the hair falls out, and on the head it causes pain like fever, and the patient sneezes;
adonques saiches par ces accidens que celles matieres et cil catharre ne vient fuer que de maintes voines, et li muedre cure que i est, si est ceste.	then you can understand from these symptoms that those matters and that catarrh do not come from just one vein, and if the treatment affects what is there, this is it.
Et est que tu comande au malaide a rere son front, puis fai une grant fendure emmi lou front, et une autre dou large I poc.	And it is that you instruct the patient to lie with their back against the wall, then make a large incision across the forehead, and another on the side of the head.
Et comence des la fendure de la temple senestre a la temple destre, et soit li incision jusc’a l’os;	And start from the left temple to the right temple, and let the incision reach to the bone;
et esloigne ta main des ners des temples que muevent au mengier;	and keep your hand away from the nerves of the temples that move during eating;
et quant li os est descovers, si essue tout le sanc a une esponge, et puis desevre entre les II levres de la fendure et i met coton viel, et tentes de lin;	and when the bone is exposed, wipe all the blood with a sponge, and then separate between the two lips of the incision and place old cotton there, and bandage with linen;
puis lie desus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile, et te garde d’aposteme chaut;	Then apply cloths soaked in wine and oil above it, and guard against hot abscesses;
quant il est ostez, si covient que tu frottes l’os tant que chars i comence a naistre, puis le cure de choses exiccatives, que font enjanrer char.	When it is removed, you must rub the bone until flesh begins to grow, then treat with substances that promote growth of flesh.
En teil maniere:	In such a manner:
pren II parties de flor de froment, et de colofoine IIII parties, et en fai emplaustre;	Take two parts of wheat flour, and four parts of colophony, and make a plaster;
et l’aministre en ces plaies por enjanrer char per tout.	and apply it to the wounds to promote flesh growth throughout.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	of the congestion of the ears
Tout ceu que chiet ens oreilles est une des IIII choses:	All that falls into the ears is one of the four things:
ou grains, ou beste, ou piere de mine ou semblans chose si com fer;	For seeds, for beasts, for stones from mines, or similar things such as iron;
ou semence, si com jaisses, feves, pois;	for seed, such as beans, peas;
ou chose defluans si com aigue et aisilz et semblans choses.	for things that flow out, such as water and saliva and similar things.
Quant il chiet en l’oreille piere ou autre maniere de chose que ne s’ajoste mie a l’oreille, ne ne croist en l’oreille, si met l’oreille au solel.	When a stone or other substance that does not belong in the ear falls into it and does not grow within the ear, place the ear towards the sun.
Se tu vois la piere, si distille aucun poc d’oile violet ou oile de sisament, puis i amenistre extraction;	If you see the stone, then drip some drops of violet oil or cumin oil, then proceed with its extraction;
et lou fai esternuer de condisi, et li estoupe les narines quant li esternuemens vient, et met entor l’oreille pieces de drapelz ou laine;	and make them sneeze with something spicy, and plug their nostrils when the sneezing comes, and place around the ear pieces of cloth or wool;
et estent l’oreille au desus.	and cover the ear above.
Mout de fois vient fuer par ceste cure;	Much fire comes from this treatment;
et s’elle ne vient fuer, se li amenistre extraction as pinceures subtilz, de coi ci est li forme:	and if it does not come with fire, then use subtle pinching to extract it, as follows:
S’elle saut fuer as pinceures, c’est boin;	If it comes out with the forceps, that is good;
se ceu non, si amenistre extraction a l’oncine subtil de petite doubleure;	if not, then extract it with a fine double-pointed instrument;
et s’elle ne saut par ceu, si fai une caine d’arain et boute lou chief de la cainne ou pertuis de l’oreille fort, et estoupe ceu qui est entor la cainne de cire mole si que li vens n’i puisse entrer avec la cainne;	and if it does not come out with that, then make a linen cord and insert the end of the cord through the hole in the ear firmly, and plug what is around the cord with soft wax so that no air can enter with the cord;
puis le trai fuer forment, car mout de fois vient fuer si com nos avons dit;	then pull it out forcefully, as it often comes out as we have said;
et s’elle ne vient fuer en teil maniere, si prent glut de coi en prent les oisiaus, et met en som aucun estrument qui soit a point por ceu faire, et met un poc de coton entor;	and if it does not come forth in such a manner, take glue as birds use, and place some instrument that is sharp for this purpose, and put a little cotton around;
puis presse le glut sus la piere ou quel chose que ce soit, et trai fuer.	then press the glue onto the stone or whatever it may be, and pull forth.
Et s’elle ne saut fuer de toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si te haste de fendre l’oreille ainsois que aposteme chalz i veigne, et spasme;	And if it does not come forth from all the things we have mentioned, then hurry to cut the ear as for an abscess so that blood may flow and spasms stop;
et li maniere de la fendure si est que tu faices premier sainier lou malaide de la cephalique, et estrai dou sanc selonc la mesure de sa vertu, puis fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains et li torne l’oreille au desus, et fent une petite fendure en la racine de l’oreille a la graisse ou leu dependant;	and the manner of the cut is that you first bleed the patient from the cephalic vein, and draw out blood according to the measure of their strength, then have the patient sit between your hands and turn the ear upwards, and make a small incision at the root of the ear in the fat where it hangs;
et soit li fendure ausi com une lune, tant que tu viegnes a la piere, puis l’oste selonc ton pooir, et la suce hastanment a ta bouche;	and let the incision be like a crescent moon, so that you come to the stone, then remove it according to your power, and suck it quickly with your mouth;
et la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and continue the treatment until he is well.
Et se c’est grains qui est ens et il enfle, si aministre extraction;	And if it is a grain that has entered and causes swelling, then proceed with its removal;
et si’il ne puet issir, si amenistre I spatumile tenve subtil selonc ceste forme:	and if it cannot come out, then proceed with the application of a thin poultice according to this form:
et amenistre incision de celui grain.	and administer an incision of that tumor.
Mais ne faire mie ceu quant tu penses que li grains est moistes por la moistor de l’oreille, tant que tu en aies fait maintes pieces;	But do not do this when you think the grain is moist due to the moisture of the ear, until you have done it many times;
puis l’estrai as pinceures subtilz et au succier, si com nos avons dit, si que li estractions soit aligie.	then extract it with fine forceps and with suction, as we have said, so that the extraction is gentle.
En l’aigue donques que chiet en l’oreille covient que li malaides use d’esternuement de condisi premiers, et ample l’oreille de viel coton.	In the case of water that falls into the ear, the patient should use sneezing to dislodge it initially, and plug the ear with old cotton.
Et soit gisans sus celle oreille meisme ou li aigue est.	And lie down on the side where the water is in the ear.
s’elle saut fuer per ceu, c’est boin.	if it falls out because of that, it is good.
se ceu non, si prent maintes pieres selonc li longesce de ton doit tenves et legieres, et les eschaufe un poc au feu;	if not, take many stones according to the length of your thumb and light, and heat them a little in the fire;
et em mette li malaides une ou pertus de son oreille, et saille sus i. de ses piez d’autre part, et fiere d’une autre piere sus la piere qui est en l’oreille;	and place them in one or a hole of his ear, and have him step on one from the other side, and strike another stone against the stone that is in the ear;
et ne cesse de faire ceu de piere em piere tant que li aigue isse toute fuer, et ensi saut elle toute fuer;	and do not stop striking stone against stone until the water flows out completely, and thus it will flow out entirely;
et se tu vues, si prent I jonc, et boute l’un des chiés en l’oreille, et l’autre chief emprent de feu tant que li plus dou jonc soit ars;	and if you wish, take some reeds, and insert one end into the ear, and burn the other end with fire until the softer part of the reed is burned;
puis refai autreteil d’autres jons tant que li aigue isse toute, si com nos avons dit en la piere.	then do the same with other reeds until the water flows out completely, as we have said about the stones.
En l’estraction de la beste, s’elle est de petit cors, si com puce et semblans chose, cure la si com nos avons dit en la division;	In the extraction of the beast, if it is a small body, such as a flea and similar things, treat it as we have said in the division;
mais s’elle est de grant cors c’on la puisse sentir, si amenistre extraction de pinceures;	but if it is large and can be felt, then treat the extraction with tweezers;
et c’est li chose plus legiere a oster qui soit en l’oreille.	and it is the lightest thing to remove that can be in the ear.
En l’estraction des vers enjanrez as oreilles, quant tu lou cures si com nos avons dit en la division et ou traitier des distillations, et li cure ne profite mie, si covient que tu regardes l’oreille au soleil:	In the extraction of worms in the ears, when you treat them as we have said in the division and in the treatment of distillations, and if the treatment does not help, then it is necessary that you look at the ear in the sun:
s’il i apert nulz vers, si les trai as pinceures subtilz, et s’il n’aperent, si prent la cainne de coi ci est li forme:	if you see any worms, then remove them with fine tweezers, and if none are seen, then take the chain of this form:
Et soit estroite desoz et large desus.	And let it be narrow below and wide above.
Et boute lou plus subtil chief en l’oreille selonc la quantiteit de la soffrance dou malaide, puis succe forment a tot la caine;	And insert the most delicate tip into the ear according to the extent of the patient's pain, then proceed gently along the entire canal;
fai ceu sovent tant que tuit li ver issent.	Do this repeatedly until all the wax comes out.
Et s’il n’obeissent a issir, si estoupe entor la cainne de coton si com j’ai dit en la piere;	And if they do not come out, plug the canal with cotton as I said for stones;
et s’il ne saillent fuer si com nos avons dit, si aministre distillations que li ancien ont esprovees en l’ocision des vers, et tu les troveras ou traitier des distillations;	and if they do not emerge as we have said, administer distillations that the ancients have tested for killing worms, and you will find them in the section on distillations;
et si distille tes oiles et tes medicines en l’oreille a tout cest estrument, de coi ci est li forme si com tu vois:	and if you distill your oils and medicines into the ear with all this equipment, of which here is the form as you see:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain estrois desoz a I petis pertuis, et desus overs por distiller;	And let it be of silver or brass narrow with small holes, and above cover to drip through;
et por presser dedens la distillation a I estrument d’arain bien fait por ceu, et se tu vues pren I raseur et envoloupe entor la pointe avenanment coton;	and to press inside the distillation use an instrument of brass well made for this, and if you wish take a scraper and wrap around the tip appropriately with cotton;
puis i giete ton oile ou ton jus, et ceu que tu vues de tes medicines en la cainne, et li caine soit en l’oreille;	then pour your oil or juice, and whatever medicine you wish into the tube, and the tube should be in the ear;
puis boute dedens lou raseur a tout lou coton, et presse ta main tempreement tant que li oile soit distilleit ou chevement de l’oreille;	then press into the scraper on all the cotton, and squeeze your hand gently until the oil is dripping into the ear canal;
et lou sente li malaides dedens, et soit li distillations I poc eschaufee au feu ainsois c’on la distille en l’oreille;	and the patient should feel it inside, and let the dripping be slightly warmed over fire so that it drips into the ear;
et garde qu’elle ne soit trop froide, car li medicine ne seroit mie si bone.	and ensure that it is not too cold, for the medicine would not be so good.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	of the congestion of the ears
Aucun enfant naissent qui n’ont nul pertus ens oreilles;	There are some children born who have no hole in their ears;
et ceste meisme chose avient as homes par estoupement de plaie, ou de char nee dedens l’oreille, et cist estoupemens vient aucune fois em parfont en l’oreille, si c’on ne lou puet veoir;	and this same thing happens to adults due to a blocked wound or flesh inside the ear, and these blockages sometimes occur deeply in the ear, so that one cannot see them;
et aucune fois avient I poc defuer lou pertus, et lou voit om bien.	and sometimes the hole is clearly visible and can be seen well.
Celle donques que vient em parfont, si c’on ne la puet veoir, est de grief sanation em plusors dispositions, et en cele c’on voit covient que tu mettes l’oreille dou malaide au soleil;	That which occurs deep inside and cannot be seen is difficult to treat in many cases, and for the one that can be seen, you should place the ear of the patient in the sun;
et regarde dedens:	and look inside:
se tu vois l’opilation apparent, si la oevre a tot cest spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	if you see the scab clearly, then perform this entire spatulation as described in its form:
Et soit agus et trenchans devant et derrier tout plain, si qu’il ne blece l’oreille;	And let it be sharp and cutting in front and behind all flat, so as not to catch the ear;
se li opilation est de char nee ou cors de l’oreille, si la tien as pinceures subtilz, et la cope legierement, tant que celle chars soit toute ostee.	if the scab is of flesh from the ear's body, then hold it with fine forceps and gently scrape it away until all the flesh is removed.
Et se li opilations est em parfont en l’oreille, si pren I raseur subtil legier et l’eschaufe un petit au feu, puis li met ou cors de l’oreille.	And if the obstruction is in the ear, take a fine, light scraper and heat it slightly over fire, then place it in the flesh of the ear.
Se tu sens l’opilation dont li malaides sent grieteit a l’oïr, perce legierement, et garde que tu ne grever les ners de l’oreille;	If you feel the scab where the patient feels pain in the ear, gently pierce it, and be careful not to injure the nerves of the ear;
puis met en l’oreille une tente selonc la largesce dou pertus, et la moille en l’oignement egyptien.	then place a dressing in the ear according to the width of the opening, and moisten it with Egyptian ointment.
Fai ceu aucun jor tant que li plaie soit soudee, ou tu pren une tente et la moille en aigue rose, et poudre sus vitriole broiet;	Do this on some day when the wound is sealed, or take a tent and moisten it with rose water, and sprinkle powdered vitriol ground;
et se tu vois enflee l’oreille, si couvient que tu traies la tente et remue une autre tente moillie en cerote qui soit fait d’oile roset et de cire, tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	and if you see the ear swollen, then it is necessary to draw out the tent and move another tent moistened in cerate made of rose oil and wax, until the swelling is removed;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it until it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si plonge une esponge et drapelz en aigue froide, et le met sus l’oreille, et use d’autres cures qui oste lou decorrement de sanc qui sont ou traitier des destillations.	And if bleeding occurs, dip a sponge and cloths in cold water, and place them on the ear, and use other treatments that stop the bleeding which are in the treatment of distillations.
de la char des papieres	of the flesh of papers
Cist althelul que vienent em papieres des eulz quant ils sont moiste et sont sec, si covient que tu les estendes de tenailles et de pinceures, et le cope d’un spatumile de ses racines;	This althæa that comes in paper from the eyes when they are moist and dry, it is necessary to stretch them with tweezers and forceps, and cut a piece from its root with a spatula;
puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet.	then place over the area vitriol ground.
Et se sans en decort, si le cauterize dou cautere lenticulaire subtil, et li cauterizeir aprés l’incision vaut mues;	And if it does not respond to being peeled off, then cauterize with a fine lentil-shaped cautery, and after the incision, it will heal.
et maintes fois repairent, cant aucune chose demoure de lor racines;	and often they repair, when something remains of their roots;
et quant elles sont cauterizees par feu, si sont arses celles racines et ne revienent mie.	and when they are cauterized with fire, those roots are burned and do not return.
de la gresle	of the hailstones
Maintes fois vienent em papieres des eulz unes choses que semblent gresle en sa forme et en sa duresce, et por ceu est ceste maladie apelee «grandine», et est une assemblee de moistor grosse en la papiere desus et desoz;	Many times in the eyes appear things that resemble hail in form and hardness, and for this reason this disease is called "hail," and it is an assembly of thick moisture above and below the eye.
li ovraiges est telz:	The work is such:
pren warde se li grandine se muet d’une part et d’autre, et c’est legiere chose a savoir;	be wary if the kneecap moves from side to side, and it is easy to know;
fent la donques dou large, puis l’escorche de chescune partie legierement, puis la prent as pinceures, et la cope.	make an incision then gently scrape each part, then take it with the forceps, and cut.
se tu ne la pues coper sens percier un poc la papiere, si ne grieve rien au malaide;	if you cannot cut it without piercing slightly the membrane, do not worry about harming the patient;
et se li fendure est grans, si l’assemble a une costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee;	and if the wound is large, sew it together with stitches, and treat it until it heals;
et s’elle est petite, si n’i faire point de force, car li oignemens la restoure tantost et enjanre char.	and if the wound is small, do not apply pressure, for the ointment will heal it quickly and generate flesh.
Et se li grandine est dessendans au dedens de l’oreille vers la partie desus, si enverse la papiere, et estent la grandine a unes pinceures, et la cope et presse d’une part et d’autre;	And if the earwax is inside the ear towards the upper part, turn the paper over, and extract the wax with forceps, and cut and press from both sides;
et se li papiere est esloignie par l’incision, ce ne grieve rien;	and if the paper is distant due to the incision, it does not matter;
et quant li grandine est copee, si leive l’oil d’aigue salee, et cure le leu de ceu qui enjanre char tant que li malaides soit sanez.	and when the wax is removed, wash the ear with salt water, and treat the area with a poultice of flesh until the patient is healed.
de la graisse des eulz	of the fat of the eyes
Exinach est une graisse qui est enjanree en toiles des papieres desus, et ce avient plus as enfans c’a nules gens, et grieve mout a lor eulz, et li vienent li catharre as matinees, et ne pueent regardeir la lumiere dou soleil por ceu que les larmes se hastent a lor eulz;	Exinach is a grease that forms on the membranes inside the eyes, and this happens more to children than adults, and it causes great pain in their eyes, and they get catarrh in the mornings, and cannot look at the sun's light because tears rush to their eyes;
et por ceu se couchent il sor lor faices adés, et dorment sus, et sont lor papieres desoz lor sorcilz moistes que li enfleure et li apparance ont covert de l’exinach qui apert en l’oil.	And for this reason they lie down on their beds immediately, and sleep, and their eyelids are moist with the secretion and appearance covered by the exudate that appears in the eye.
Et quant tu presses lou leu a tes dois et sent l’exirnach entr’ous.	And when you press that place with your thumb and feel the exinach between them.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain;	And the method of the work is that the patient places their head on your hand;
et puis pren I drapeil de lin, et appareille une tente em maniere d’un cercle selonc la quantiteit que conteigne exirnach de chescune partie, puis le met sus li;	and then take a piece of linen, and prepare a tent in the manner of a circle according to the quantity that contains exudate for each part, then place it on them;
et presse a tes dois d’une part et d’autre, si que li exirnach soit assemblez emmi le cercle;	and press with your two hands from both sides so that the exudate is gathered within the circle;
puis fent em mileu de la moistor au spatumile trenchant une fendure dou large, et ne soit mie plus grans que li plaie c’on fait a la sainie de voinne;	then make in the middle of the moisture with a sharp spatula a narrow incision, and let it not be larger than the wound made when opening a vein;
et fent le cuir em parfont tant que tu veignes a l’exirnach;	and they cut the skin deeply until you reach the external part;
et em plusors dispositions vient exirnach de la fendure, selonc la forme d’une piece de graisse blainche.	and in many positions, the external part comes from the fissure, according to the form of a piece of white fat.
Estrai la donques a tout une piece de drap charpit entre tes dois au defuer, et torne ta main a destre et a senestre tant qu’il soit espars;	Extract it then in one piece of torn cloth between your two hands, and move your hand right and left until it is spread out;
et garde que tu n’ajoster en la fendure, que tu ne viegnes a tout le spatumile jusc’a l’oil, que tu ne le bleces.	and be careful not to insert anything into the fissure, do not touch the entire spatumile until the eye, and do not injure it.
Et se li exirnach n’apert en l’encomencement de la fendure, si acroi un poc la fendure legierement tant qu’il apere;	And if the external part does not appear at the beginning of the fissure, then slightly enlarge the fissure gently until it appears;
puis l’estrai si com nos avons dit, puis moille drapelz en aisil et en aigue, et met sus le leu, et estrain de bendelz.	Then extract it as we have said, then moisten cloths in wine and water, and place them on the site, and extract bandages.
Et si a de tels homes qui broient seil et mettent sus por corrompre cele moistor qui est demoree.	And there are such people who grind salt and put it on to corrupt the moisture that remains.
Puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat him until he is well.
Et s’il vient au leu aposteme chaut, si lou cure d’emplaustres assouajant tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if it comes to the place of an abscess being hot, treat him with plasters that soothe until he is well.
des poilz des papieres	of the hair of the eyelids
Quant em papieres naissent poilz ajostez autre que li naturez, et sont enveillit, si nuisent as eulz, et font venir manieres de maladies si com larmes acostumees et mollifications des papieres et albugine, tant que c’est cause de la destruction des eulz;	When hairs grow in places other than those designated by nature on the eyelids, and they are not removed, they harm the eyes and cause certain ailments such as habitual tears and inflammation of the eyelids and conjunctiva, to the extent that it is the cause of the destruction of the eyes;
et est li cure selonc IIII manieres:	and the treatment follows in four ways:
ou par cautere ensamble feu, ou par medicine ague selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre de cautere, et est fais ou par incision et costure ou par caines, selonc ceu que je dirai.	either by cautery with fire altogether, or by medication as described in the chapter on cautery, and it is done either by cutting and suturing or by cantharides, as I will explain.
Il covient que tu mettes lou chief dou malaide en ton sain, puis torne la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre;	It is necessary for you to place the head of the patient on your thigh, then turn the palm of the eye toward your left hand;
s’elle est convertie, c’est boin;	if it is converted, that is good;
se ceu non, si i boute une aguille a tout I fil desus;	if not, then insert a needle along the entire thread above;
et soit ce delez la marge de la papiere ou li poil naissent delez ces poilz, et trai I fil au desus a tout la papiere, et la torne au raseur;	and do this near the margin of the palm where the hair grows among these hairs, and draw the thread above across the entire palm, and then turn it to the edge;
puis fent en la partie desoz la papiere, desoz les poilz ajostez, a tout le spatumile copant, des le grant larmier jusc’au petit;	then cut in the part below the palm, below the adjacent hairs, across the entire spatium from the large tear duct to the small;
puis estrai I fil, et met desoz la papiere une petite tente de couton et de drapeil, puis seigne sus la papiere une figure d’enche, si com la fuelle de mirte, et toutevoie il covient que li figure soit selonc la quantiteit que tu vues eslever la papiere qui est devisez a toz.	Then pull out the thread, and under the paper place a small tent of cotton and linen, then draw on the paper a pattern, as the leaf of myrtle, and nonetheless it must be according to the quantity that you wish to raise the paper which is designed for all.
Et si a teil qui a mestier c’on cope grant quantiteit de la papiere selonc ceu que li papiere est mollifie;	And if there is someone who needs to cut a large quantity of the paper according to how the paper has softened;
puis fent a tout le spatumile sus les II lignes que tu as signiet, et comence des lou grant larmier jusc’a petit;	Then cut through the entire spatumile along the two lines that you have marked, and start from the large window down to the small;
et soit li une des fendures pres des poilz naturez en la groissece d’un raiz, puis boute l’oncine en l’un des II angles dou keur, puis l’escorche toute;	and let one of the cuts be near the natural hairs in the thickness of a root, then insert the needle into one of the two corners of the cautery site, then peel it all off;
puis assemble les II levres a une costure d’une aguille a tout I fil de laine subtil, et essue le sanc, et fai aerdre la superfluiteit des filz sus les II sorcilz a tout aucunes choses gluans, se tu vues faire ce;	Then join the two lips with a seam using one fine needle and a thread of thin wool, wipe away the blood, and trim any excess thread above the two eyebrows with some sticky substance if you wish to do so;
et se ce non, si n’en aies cure, puis laisse la costure et les filz jusc’a III jors ou IIII;	and if you do not wish to do this, then leave the seam and the threads until three or four days;
puis cure la plaie sens costure de choses sechans et constrignans, car li papiere se relive au soudement de la plaie et l’assemblement de li, mais li costure est muedre (si com dirent li ancien), et c’est ovraiges sens paor;	then treat the wound without stitching with drying and binding materials, because the paper rises suddenly at the moment of the wound and its healing, but the stitch is moved (as the ancients say), and these are works without fear;
et si a une autre maniere:	and there is another method:
et est que tu seignes la papiere d’une figure qui soit ausi com li fuelle de mirte, si com nos avons conteit, a III oncines desevrez selonc la forme qui est ci:	And it is that you should cauterize the paper with a figure that is like the leaf of myrtle, as we have described, at three inches apart according to the form which is here:
puis cope ceu qui sormonte as petites forces igalment selonc la forme qui est ci:	Then cut those which rise above the small parts equally according to the shape which is here:
Et se tu n’as pooir de tenir les tenailles, et li chose n’est mie igalz, si prent une aguille ou il ait I fil, et la boute emmi la figure;	And if you do not have the ability to hold the tongs, and the objects are not even, then take a needle with a thread, and tie it around the figure;
et boute I autre fil delez lou grant larmier, et lou secont fil delez lou petit, et assemble entre tes dois les filz igalment;	and tie another thread next to the large artery, and the second thread next to the small one, and join them equally between your two fingers;
puis lieve ta main igalment, et lieve tout le cuir sus coi tu as signiet, si com nos avons conteit, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie par costure, et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	then lift your hand evenly, and raise all the skin on which you have cauterized, as we have described, then stitch together the two edges of the wound, and treat it until it is healed;
et se aposteme vient a ton incision, si l’apaise de cerote et de semblans oignement assouajans;	And if an abscess comes to your incision, soothe it with plaster and similar soothing ointments;
et aucune fois avient que li poil de la papiere sont convertit:	And sometimes the hair on the skin is turned back:
si covient que tu uses ceu que nos avons dit de l’incision;	Then you should use what we have said about incision;
mais li costure en l’une et en l’autre est plus artificialz.	but the suturing in both cases is more artificial.
Li cure des caines si est selonc ceste forme:	The treatment for canes follows this form:
et est que tu convertisses la papiere et la fent dedens selonc ceu que j’ai dit, et puis fai II caines par art, et II liiens subtilz ausi lonc com li papiere et li largesce dou spatumile est;	and it is that you turn the skin and make an incision according to what I have said, and then make two canes by art, and two fine straps as long as the skin and as wide as the spatula is;
et cope as II chiés de II pars ou tu tiens les filz;	and cut to II heads of II sides where you hold the threads;
puis assemble l’un et l’autre subtilment sus ceu que sormonte de la papiere de l’oil, et estrain les II cainnes des II parties forment;	then join one to the other carefully on what protrudes from the eye's membrane, and pull apart the two threads of the two parts firmly;
et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, et li cuir qui iert estrainte morra et nercira et porrira, tant qu’il cherra par lui.	and leave it thus for some days, and the skin which is stretched will die, blacken, and pus, until it falls off on its own.
S’il tarde, si le cope a unes forces, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	If it delays, cut it with force, then treat it until it is healed;
et quant li plaie iert soudee, et si ert levee li papiere, et ne poindront plus li poil;	and when the wound is closed, and the membrane raised, the hairs will no longer prick;
et c’est li forme des II cainnes que tu feras selonc ceste figure, et selonc ceste quantiteit de lonc et de large:	and this is the form of the two threads that you will make according to this figure, and according to this length and width:
li ovraiges est telz que tu preignes une aguille subtil, et i boute I fil de soie souef et subtil;	The work is such that you take a fine needle, and put a thin and fine silk thread through it;
puis assemble les chiés et noe l’un et l’autre subtilment, et soit li longesce des filz une palme de lonc;	then join the heads and tie them together carefully, and let the length of the thread be one palm;
puis ordene en la chasse I autre fil subtil de soie briément, et noe les chief dou fil;	then arrange another fine silk thread briefly in the wound, and tie the ends of the thread gently;
puis mette li malaides son chief en ton sain;	then have the patient place his head on your shoulder;
et soit delez lou soleil si que li ovraiges soit declairiez, car c’est uns ovraiges subtilz et menus, puis boute l’aguille a tout la chasse en la racine dou poil ajosteit, et la fai percier en la papiere hastanment tant que tu la traies desus lou poil natureil;	and let it be near the sun so that the work is clearly visible, for this is a delicate and precise task; then insert the needle throughout the wound at the root of the adjacent hair, and pierce through the membrane quickly as you draw it over the natural hair;
puis estrai le poil jusque sus la chasse, et boute en la chasse celui poil, s’il en i a I ou II ou III ou plusors;	Then pluck out the hair up to the root, and insert back that hair if there are one or two or three or more;
puis estrai ta main tant que li poilz veigne fuers a tout la chasse en la papiere avec lou poil natureil.	Then pull out your hand until the hairs come completely out of the root along with the natural hair.
Et se li chasse est traite et li poilz ne vient fuer avec li, si trairas la chasse au desoz a tout le fil que tu i as ordeneit, tant que li chasse veigne fuer dou pertus desus et que tu la voies par la vision de l’oil;	And if the root is tight and the hairs do not come out with them, then draw the root from behind along the thread you have inserted until the root comes out of the opening above and you can see it with your eye;
adonques si trairas la chasse et le fil, et clo l’oil et lou laisse clo II jors ou III, tant que li poil s’aerde en son leu et naisse li char sus;	then draw out the root and the thread, and close the eye and leave it closed for two or three days until the hair grows in its place and flesh grows over;
et se li poilz est petis, si acompaigne I poil lonc des chevoulz naturez, et soit alevez avec celui ou tu le laisse, tant qu’il soit eslongiez et puis le lieve.	And if the hairs are short, match one long hair with natural hair, and lift it up along with those you leave, so that it is raised and then take it.
de la porriture de l’oil	from the pus of the eye
Quant ceste maladie qui est apelee «aleacrati» ou li porriture vient en l’oil, si en i a de II manieres:	When this disease called "aleacrati" or putridity comes to the eye, there are two ways it can occur:
l’une natureil, et l’autre innatureil.	one naturally, and the other unnaturally.
Et avient par soudement de plaie, ou de tailleure ou de cautere, et par semblans choses.	And it happens by sudden wound, or cutting, or cauterizing, and similar things.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige en li est que tu fendes celle soudure, et dessevre les levres de li, et met dedens tentes de lin, et la lie tant qu’elle soit sanee;	And the method of treatment is that you cut open the seam, and separate the lips of it, and put in linen tents, and keep it raised until it heals;
et ne covient mie que tu uses en la cure de li de choses que sechent et restraignent.	and you must not use in the treatment of it things that dry and constrict.
Car se tu fais ceu, si revient li maladie pire que li premiere;	For if you do this, the illness returns worse than before;
mais i oevre de choses amollissans, si com fenugreic;	but use things that soften, such as fenugreek;
et l’arose d’aigue ou altee et semence de lin soient cuites, et oignemens dyaquilon fondut en aucun des oiles, et i envoloupe une tente, et le cure de ceu.	and boil the water of hellebore and flax seeds, and mix the melted cerate with some oil, then wrap a dressing in it, and treat him with this.
Et li tresors de ta cure si est que tu te dones en garde qu’ele ne soude mie selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant;	And the goal of your treatment is to ensure that it does not heal according to its former shape;
et cist ovraiges que nos avons dit nen est fuers que adresemens de ceste maladie, qu’elle ne reviegne selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant.	and these treatments we have mentioned are nothing but methods to prevent this illness from returning to its former shape.
de la char qui vient en l’oil	of the flesh that comes into the eye
Ceste maladie que est desoz qui vraiement est apelee «axacrati», et est naturelz et accidens.	This disease which is called "axacrati" in truth, and it is both natural and accidental.
Li accidens vient de plaie et de fendure et de cautere et de choses semblans;	The accident comes from a wound and a cut and a cautery and similar things;
et li voie de l’ovraige en li si est que tu preignes un aguille, en coi il ait I fil double, et la fiche en la char, et li fai percier des le senestre larmier tant c’a destre, si que li filz veigne en II chiés de la char;	and the method of the work is that you take a needle, in which there is double thread, and insert it into the flesh, and make it pierce from the left cheekbone to the right, so that the thread comes out in two places on the skin;
puis estent la char au desus a tout l’aguille, et la cope a I spatumile large.	then stretch the flesh above completely over the needle, and cover it with a piece of cloth about an inch wide.
Et se li figure de la papiere revient selonc ceu qu’il covient, c’est boin;	And if the shape of the paper returns as it should, that is good;
se ceu non, si pren I raseur et le met en la fendure, et torne la papiere, et fent II fendures ou costeit dedens la papiere;	if not, then take a scraper and place it in the cut, and turn the paper, and make two cuts inside the paper;
et soient li chiés des II fendures des II angles de l’incision que tu as copeit, et soit fais uns angles si que quant elles sont assemblees, que li figure soit ausi com li figure d’une lettre qui a non «I griesche»;	and let the head of the two grooves at the two corners of the incision you have made be in such a way that when they are assembled, the shape should be like the letter called "X" Greek;
puis oste celle char, selonc la quantiteit que ses costez est agus desoz, de ceu qui enseut la papiere, puis ajoste les II parties desevrees, et les cout d’un fil de lainne;	then remove the flesh according to the sharpness of its edges from that which is under the paper, then join the two separated parts together with a thread of wool;
puis lou cure de ceu que nos avons dit des medicines mollifians, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat with what we have said about softening remedies and tents until he is healed.
Et se li maladie vient de fendure ou de costure ou de cautere, si covient que tu fendes une fendure plainne desoz les poilz des papieres, et selonc ceu qui est ci devant;	And if the illness comes from a wound or suture or cauterization, then you must cut an open incision under the hair of the paper area, and as described above;
puis desevre entre les II leivres d’une tente, si com j’ai dit;	Then separate between the two leaves of a tent, as I have said;
et doit on faire l’ovraige selonc la forme de la maladie, car elle est mout diverse en forme, et li saiges maistres appareille engien de tout som pooir coment il faice revenir la figure a sa forme natureil;	and one must perform the work according to the form of the illness, for it is very diverse in form, and wise masters prepare remedies with all their power as they should restore the figure to its natural form;
et li malaides meisme, selonc ceu qu’il i covient d’ovraige et d’estrumens em plusors dispositions.	and the patient himself, according to what is required of work and instruments in various circumstances.
dou soudement de la papiere	of the sudden swelling of the skin
Quant ceste soudure avient a mains homes en teil maniere que li papiere desus est sodee avec le blanc de l’oil, et ne puet movoir ne faire ses ovraiges naturez, si covient donques que tu i boutes la pointe d’un raseur desoz la papiere, et la lieve en haut;	When this adhesion occurs in some people such that the membrane above is adhered to the white of the eye, and they cannot move or perform their natural actions, then you should insert the tip of a razor below the membrane, and lift it up;
et l’estent as pinceures, tant que tu copes ceu qui est aert au spatumile subtil, qui ne soit mie trop agus ne trop trenchans, si que li malaides ne puisse soffrir que li spatumile trop agus ne blecent l’oil;	and place the tweezers, such that you cut what is adhered to the thin spatula, which must not be too sharp or too cutting, so that the patient cannot bear for the overly sharp spatula to hurt the eye;
et soit ton incision, dont tu escorche celle assemblee, legierement, si que li papiere reviegne selonc sa forme natureil;	and let your incision, by which you peel off that assembly, be slight, so that the tissue returns according to its natural form;
et est sanee toute celle assemblee, et font aucune fois en l’oil aigue salee, et le leve d’aigue douce, et de coliere;	and when that entire assembly is healed, sometimes they treat the eye with salt water, and lift it with gentle water, and use poultices;
puis met entre la papiere et l’oil une tente de lin, et met sus l’oil laine moillie en abun d’uef;	then place between the tissue and the eye a tent of linen, and put on the eye wool moistened abundantly with egg;
et aprés le tier jor use dou coliere et des choses soudans tant qu’il soit sanez.	And after the third day, use a colic belt and solid foods until he is well.
de l’ungle de l’oil	of the nail of the eye
Saiches que li ungle est selonc II manieres:	Know that the nail grows in two ways:
elle est nervouse et semblans a I dur syfac, et une autre qui n’est mie nervouse, mais est semblans a blainche moistor congelee, que quant on la touche de fer et on la cuide panre as pinceures, si ne puet om;	it is nervous and similar to hard fat, and another which is not nervous, but is like frozen white moisture, such that when one touches it with iron and thinks to cut it with pliers, it cannot be done;
et l’une et l’autre semblance encomence devers le grant larmier, et croist poc et poc tant qu’ele cuevre toute la veue et toute la lumiere et le movement de l’oil.	and both of these conditions start near the large tear duct and grow little by little until they cover the entire vision, light, and movement of the eye.
Et li maniere de l’incision si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz;	And the method of incising is that the patient should place their head on your lap, then you work on their eyes;
et lieve la papiere a ta main, puis coil l’ungle as pinceures de petite doubleure, et l’estent au desus;	and lift the paper with your hand, then curl the nail at the edges of thin leather, and place it above;
puis pren une aguille, et i met I poil de cheval, ou de vaiche, ou de buef, et I fil fort;	then take a needle, and put horsehair, or goat hair, or ox hair on it, and strong thread;
et double la pointe de l’aguille un poc et la fiche emmi l’ungle, et la perce a tout l’aguille, et lie l’ungle d’un fil et l’estent au desus, et escorche a tout lou poil le costeit de l’ungle qui enseut la prunele et la soie au poil jusc’au chief, puis cope lou remanant en la racine dou larmier a tout lou spatumile subtil et as petites forces, et laisse la char natureil ou larmier, si que par l’incision ne veigne li cors des larmes acostumeement;	and double the tip of the needle a little and insert it under the nail, and pierce through with the entire needle, and tie the nail with thread and place it above, and shave all around the side of the nail that contains the plumule and the hair to the top, then cut the remaining part at the root of the nail very finely and with small force, leaving the natural flesh of the nail so that by the incision no skin tears accustomedly;
et aucune fois s’estent li ungle a l’oncine soulement, et au fil, si com nos avons dit;	and sometimes the nail adheres solely to the bone, and with a thread, as we have said;
puis l’escorche on a tout le spatumile souef de coi ci est li forme:	then the skin is stripped off all of the spatumile, which is as follows in form:
Et garde que li spatumile ne touche la toile charnue et la rompe, et que li prunele ne soit percie;	And be careful that the spatumile does not touch the tender flesh and tear it, and that the probe is not pierced;
et aprés l’incision giete en l’oil un poc de seil broiet, et dou coliere fait de litargire, et le laisse jusc’a l’autre jor;	and after the incision, sprinkle a bit of ground sulfur and a preparation made from litharge into the eye, and leave it until the next day;
puis le cure de ceu qu’il i covient tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it as necessary until it is healed.
Et se li ungle n’est mie nervouse, et tu ne pues bouter l’aguille, et li uncines n’i puet entrer, maintes fois est curee ceste semblance d’ungle de medicines;	And if the nail is not loose and you cannot insert the needle, and the probe cannot enter, this condition of the nail is often treated with various medicines;
et naissent sicom j’ai conteit en la division, et se tu la vues coper, si oevre l’oil dou malaide, et pren le spatumile legier poc agut selonc ceste forme:	and they grow as I have described in the division, and if you wish to cut them, let the patient's eye observe, and take a spatula gently and quickly according to this form:
Et reis l’ungle desus subtilment, et se tu vois qu’elle amenuise point et li rasion i apresse, si distille de ta bouche en l’oil coliere fait de litargire et dou coliere rouge et seil broiet, et estoupe l’oil jusc’a l’autre jor;	And lift the eyelid gently, and if you see it shrink slightly and the reason presses on it, then drop from your mouth into the eye a solution made of litharge and red chalk finely ground, and plug the eye until the next day;
puis rencomence l’autre ovraige selonc ceste meisme oevre, tant qu’elle soit toute ostee.	then begin the other work according to this same method, until it is all removed.
Se aucune chose ne t’est contraire en l’oil, si com aposteme chaus, adonques la lait, et cure premier l’aposteme chaut tant qu’il soit sanez, puis rencomence l’ovraige si com devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.	If anything is contrary in the eye, such as a hot abscess, then stop, and treat the hot abscess until it is healed, then resume the work as before, until it is healed.
Et se li apparance de la chair dou larmier nuit en l’oil par grant nuisement, si la sospent a l’oncine, et en cope une partie et non mie tot, que cors de larmes n’i viegne;	And if the appearance of the flesh of the eyelid harms the eye greatly, then suspend it to the nail, and cut part of it but not all, so that no more tears come forth;
puis distille en l’oil coliere rouge qui est fais de litargire.	Then sprinkle into the eye a red solution made from litharge.
de la char qui naist sus la prunelle	of the flesh that grows over the pupil
Es eulz d’aucuns homes naist aucune fois char rouge, et cuevre la prunele et restraint sus les papieres et les torne au defuer, et semble une rose de balauste;	In some people's eyes, a red substance sometimes appears, covering the pupil and restraining it over the whites, turning it outward, and it looks like a rose petal.
et li ovraiges si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz, et coil toute celle char as uncines convenaubles a ceu, et la sostien a la force;	And the procedure is that the patient places their head on your lap, then you work on their eyes, and carefully remove all that red substance with appropriate hooks, and support it with strength;
puis cope la premiere char, et vai tout copant au raseur jusc’a la fin, et te garde que tu ne bleces l’oil a l’ovraige;	Then cut the first layer of tissue, and keep cutting with the scalpel until the end, and be careful not to injure the eye during the procedure;
et soit li incision dou spatumile que nos avons dit en l’incision de l’ungle et as petites forces de coi on oste lou sebel, si com li forme aprés cest chapistre lou demostre;	And let the incision be made with a spatula, as we described for cutting nails and removing small pieces, as the form following this chapter demonstrates;
et quant li incision est acomplie et ostee toute li char, si emple l’oil de seil broiet ou tu i distille coliere rouge et semblans medicines corrosives, et met sus l’oil defuer coton avec abin d’uef, si qu’il soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut;	And when the incision is complete and all the flesh is removed, then apply the juice of boiled rue or pour on red colic water and similar corrosive medicines, and place over it cotton soaked in egg white so that it is secure from hot abscess.
et s’il i demore rien, et li sans chaus te sormonte, et tu doutes aposteme chaut, si laisse l’oil et cure l’aposteme de choses apaisant aposteme chaut;	And if anything remains and the blood flows up, and you fear a hot abscess, then leave the medicine and treat the hot abscess with soothing remedies.
puis revien a ton ovraige tant qu’il soit sanez, et ensi fai cant chars est ajostee en l’oil par ceste semblance.	Then return to your work until it is healed, and thus do when flesh is applied to the eye in this manner.
Mais toutevoie il covient que tu aliges la cure de chescun oil foible de la voie natureil;	However, it is necessary that you lighten the treatment of each weak eye according to the natural way;
et de la voie accident, en ovraige de fer;	and from accidental injury, in work with iron;
et ne bouter mie ta main en aucun de ces ovraiges tant que tu voies que cist membres soit soffrans celui ovraige.	and do not put your hand into any of these works until you see that this member can endure the work.
des voines des eulz	of the veins of the eyes
Sebel sont voinnes rouges que sont covertes sus l’oil, et tolent a la veue son ovraige et afoiblissent l’oil toz jors.	Blood vessels are red and are covered over the eye, and their appearance weakens the sight and weakens the eye all day.
Mestier est donques au premier que tu regardes se li oil, en coi sebel est, est fors, et n’i a autre maladie fuers que lou sebel;	Therefore, first you must check if the eye, in which the ulcer is, is protruding, and there is no other disease except for the ulcer;
adonques le coil en teil maniere:	then treat it as follows:
comande au malaide qu’il mette son chief en ton sain, puis sospent celles voines a tout l’oncine selonc sa sapience, et soit li oncines subtilz double selonc ceste forme:	instruct the patient to place his head in your lap, then suspend those veins along the arm according to your knowledge, and let the veins be fine doubled according to this form:
Et soient dui oncine par degrez en I cors selonc ceste forme:	And let two incisions be made step by step on the body according to this form:
puis c’on coil as forces celles voinnes subtilment, et essue lou sanc houre aprés autre, tant que tu voies removoir celles voines fuers de l’oil;	then when you treat the veins with force gently, and wipe the blood hour after another, until you see the veins move away from the eye;
et garde que tu ne blecier l’oil as pointes des spatumiles, et fai cest ovraige a houre de midi devant lou soleil, et soies mout fervans en ton ovraige si que tu ne copes fuer que celles voinnes;	And be careful not to strike the eye with the points of the spatulae, and perform this work at noon in front of the sun, and be very zealous in your work so that you do not miss any veins;
et quant tu avras ce fait, si distille en l’oil coliere vert et rouge por corrumpre ceu qui est demorez dou sebel.	And when you have done this, then apply green and red collyrium to the eye to dissolve what remains of the cataract.
Et se tu n’as pooir de coillir tout ceu en celle houre, si fai emplastre sus l’oil de choses apaisans la dolor des eulz, et le laisse aucuns jors tant que li dolors soit apaisie et soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut, puis rencomence selonc ceste maniere qui est devant tant qu’il soit sanez;	And if you do not have the ability to collect everything at that hour, then apply a poultice to the eye with things that alleviate the pain of the eyes, and leave it for several days until the pain is relieved and there is assurance of no hot abscess, then resume according to this manner as described above until he is healthy.
et c’est li forme des forces:	and this is the form of the forces:
de la fistule de l’oil	Of the fistula of the eye
Li mire si nomment «arissati» fistule:	The physician calls this type of ulcer "arissati":
quant tu la cures per cautere et par medicine ague ardant selonc ceu que j’ai devant dit, et elle n’est mie sanee, si est engien en li que tu fendes sus l’aposteme, lai ou il doit meurer, et trai toute la moistor que i est, tant que li os soit descovers.	when you treat it with cautery and hot medicines as I have said before, and it does not heal, then there is pus that you must incise at the abscess, where it should be opened, and drain all the moisture that is inside, until the bone is exposed.
Et quant li os iert descovers, et tu verras la corruption et la noiror, si la reis a tout l’estrument de coi ci est li forme;	And when the bone is exposed, and you see the corruption and blackness, then remove it with all the instruments of which this is the form;
et est apelez «aspre chief», et soit fait de feir inde a I chief reont, et soit pointoiez si com une lime si com il est en la presente forme:	and it is called "aspre chief", and it should be made of iron for the head to be blunt, and it should be pointed like a file as shown in the present form:
Et met sus lou leu de l’os corrumput, puis le torne entre tes dois, et presse ta main un poc tant que tu saiches que celle corruption est rese;	And place it on the site of the corrupted bone, then turn it between your two fingers, and press your hand a little until you know that the corruption is resolved;
et fai ceu aucune fois, puis restoure lou leu de medicines exiccatives.	and do this several times, then restore the site with drying medications.
se li leus est soudez, et char i naist, et li cors de la bowe est soudez, et remaint ensi XL jors, et il ne renovele et n’est mie apostemez, et accidens mavais n’i vient, saiches qu’il est sanez;	if the flesh is sealed and new flesh grows, and the body of the bone is sealed, and it remains thus for forty days, and it does not renew itself and is not inflamed or infected, then you know that it is healed;
se ceu non, si n’i a autre engien que de ramener la fistule au pertus dou neif selonc ceste forme:	if not, then there is another cause to bring the fistula to the navel opening according to this form:
et est que tu descuevre de l’os la seconde fois par fer, et par medicines agues, et quant il iert descovers si prent I foret selonc ceste forme, et soit li chiés de fer a III angles, et li fust soit atenuis jusc’a chief si com tu vois ci:	and it is that you uncover the bone for the second time with an instrument and with wet medicines, and when it is uncovered take one forefinger according to this form, and let the tip of the iron be at three angles, and the shaft should be slender until the end as shown here:
puis le met sus l’os delez lou larmier, et esloigne ta main de l’oil I poc, puis torne a tot le foret tant qu’il perce l’os et le sent li malaides par ceu que li vens en ist s’il tient sa main sus son neif;	Then place it on the bone near the cheekbone, and move your hand away from the eye one inch, then turn the probe completely until it pierces the bone and the patient feels it because the wind enters if he holds his hand on his neck;
et pues restoure lou leu de medicines seches, si com je t’ai ensigniet, et quant li char naist et endurcist li leus, si vait li matiere au neif;	and then restore the place with dry medications as I have taught you, and when the flesh grows and hardens the area, remove the material from the neck;
si est plus legiere chose au malaide.	it is easier for the patient.
de l’issue de l’oil	from the outlet of the eye
Quant li eulz apert fuer dou tout en tout, et il ne vient point de destorbier au nef, ne amenuisement, si covient que tu lies lou malaide;	When the eye has become completely open and there is no disturbance or reduction in vision, then you must bind the patient;
puis le saine, puis li met ventouses ou haterel sens ferir por succier, puis met sus l’oil I liien fait d’acaice et de aloe et d’encens et de sarcocolle, et puis estrain l’oil, et l’emplaustre sus de bendes et de drapelz;	then heal it, then apply cups without striking to suck, then place on the eye a bandage made of acacia and aloes and incense and myrrh, and then extract the eye, and the plaster over strips of linen and cloths;
et li maniere des drapelz si est que tu preignes drapelz assez molz, et double chescun en IIII, et puis met l’un sus l’autre selonc la quantiteit que li eulz en ait mestier;	And the method for the cloths is that you take cloths sufficiently soft, and fold each in four, and then place one on top of another according to the quantity that the eyes require.
puis l’estrain par desus d’un bendeil dur forment, et rencomence les ventouses por succier sens ferir;	Then strain them over a hard bandage form, and reuse the suction cups to suck without injuring.
puis oste les ventouses et laisse l’oil estraint jor et nuit, et se li liiens amolist, si covient que tu l’estraignes mout;	Then remove the suction cups and leave the eye held tight day and night, and if the bandages loosen, it is necessary to hold them tightly again.
puis oste lou liien aprés le jor et la nut, et se tu vois l’oil repairier, c’est boin;	Then remove the bandage after the day and night, and if you see the eye healing, it is good.
se ce non;	if not;
si rencomence l’emplaustre et les drapelz et lou liien et les ventouses tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then restart the poultice and the bandages and the ligature and the cupping until he is well.
dou derrompement de toile uvee	from the tearing of a swollen vein
Quant disruptions vient en la toile uvee, puis apert, et vient fuer des papieres si com I grain de resins, et est espoantauble a veoir;	When disruption comes to the avascular tissue, it becomes apparent, and force appears from the papers as if it were resin grains, and it is terrifying to see;
adonques se tu la vues coper, li ovraiges est telz que tu boutes une aguille en la racine des la partie desoz jusc’a celi desus, puis boute une autre aguille ou il ait I fil double des la partie dou larmier;	then if you see it needs to be cut, the procedure is such that you insert a needle into the root of the part below up to where it is above, then insert another needle where there is a double thread from the part by the eyebrow;
et la fai percier, et laisse la premiere aguille selonc la disposition;	and there you pierce it, and leave the first needle according to its position;
puis cope lou leu dou fil double et lie une partie de l’uve entor, et l’estraint bien, puis estrai l’aguille et met sus l’oil lainne moillie en abun d’uef;	then cut the place of the double thread and tie a part of the uvea around it tightly, then remove the needle and put on the eye wool moistened in abundance with egg;
et le laisse tant que li filz chiece avec l’uve, puis cure l’oil de choses confortans tant que li plaie soit sanee;	and leave it until the child falls with the grape, then treat the eye with comforting things until the wound is healed;
et aucune fois li plaie est restrainte par l’uve chescune part d’un cercle de drap, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	and sometimes the wound is restrained by the grape on each side with a circle of cloth until it is healed.
Et se li eulz done grant apparance, si le perce au spatumile subtil qui viegne em parfont de l’oil, et corre la moistor albuginé et dessende li eulz, et entre ens tantost;	And if the eye shows great appearance, then pierce it with a fine spatula that comes in perfectly from the eye, and draw out the white moisture and lower the eye, and enter it immediately;
puis l’estrai tant qu’il soit sanez.	then extract until it is healed.
de la bowe de l’oil	of the socket of the eye
Ceste maladie qui est apelee «alcunnati» nen est fuers que bowe qui est assemblee en l’oil, semblant a aigue dessendant, et ce n’est mie aigue;	This disease which is called "alcunnati" is nothing but fluid that is gathered in the eye, resembling water descending, and it is not actually water.
et li maniere de l’apparance de l’ovraige si est que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege appareilliet et droit, puis prent le chief entre tes mains de II pars, et lou muef tant que tu voies la bowe venir au desus a tes eulz;	And the manner of appearance of the work is that you seat the patient upon a prepared and straight chair, then take his head between your hands on both sides, and move it until you see the brow come up to your eyes;
puis soit ens fichie, et ne dessende et soit descombree li lumiere, et voie li malaides les choses si com il soloit;	then let it be fixed in place, and do not allow it to descend and let the light be unobstructed, so that the patient can see things as he usually would;
et s’elle ne dessent desoz, saiches que c’est aigue, et se li dessendemens de la bowe n’est appareilliez si com nos avons dit.	and if it does not descend properly, know that it is acute, and if the descent of the brow is not prepared as we have said.
si fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, puis prent le spatumile subtil et fent sus la toile cornee I poc par la continuation de la conjunctive avec la toile cornee et la corone, tant que li bowe isse;	seat the patient between your hands, then take a fine speculum and cut through the corneal membrane in one spot along the continuation of the conjunctiva with the corneal membrane and the cornea, until the brow rises;
et quant elle ert issue, si distille en l’oil aigue chaude mellee a miel, ou aigue ou fenugreic est boillis et miel, puis soit curee d’autre cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And when it comes out, drip into the eye hot honey mixed with half mead or boiling water and fenugreek, then treat it further until it is healed.
des aigues de l’oil	for the waters of the eye
Nos avons jai les semblances des aigues en la division, et ceu qu’il covient por percier;	We have described the appearances of the waters in the division, and what is necessary for piercing;
si en oevre selonc la santeit.	and act according to health.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains croisiet, fuers de la lumiere por le soleil, et li lie l’oil sain et estreint mout fort;	It is necessary that you seat the patient between your crossed hands, away from the light to shield from the sun, and hold the healthy eye tightly.
puis met la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre se li eulz est senestres, ou a ta main destre se li eulz est destres;	then place the paper of the eye on your left hand if the eye is left, or on your right hand if the eye is right;
puis prent en ta main destre, se li eulz est senestres, l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda», ou a ta main senestre, se li eulz est destre;	Then take in your right hand, if the eye is left, the instrument which is called "almagda", or in your left hand, if the eye is right;
puis met la pointe de l’estrument delez la corone par la groissece d’un rait en celle blenchor de l’oil a la partie dou menor larmier, puis boute l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda» vertuousement, et trestorne ta main tant qu’il perce en la blenchor de l’oil, et sente que almagda viegne a la chose vuide;	Then place the tip of the instrument next to the cornea by the thickness of a hair on that white part of the eye towards the inner corner, then insert the instrument called "almagda" forcefully, and turn your hand until it penetrates the white part of the eye, and feel as the almagda enters the empty space;
et covient que li mesure de la voie almagda soit au parfont de la mesure des l’espaice qui est des la prunele jusc’a la fin de la noirour;	and it is necessary that the length of the almagda be exactly equal to the space from the pupil to the end of the black part;
et c’est li corone de l’oil;	and this is the crown of the eye;
si verras l’os en celle papiere por la clarteit de la toile cornee, et pues met l’estrument jusc’a leu ou li aigue est, puis l’espresse desoz une voie aprés autre.	you will see the bone through that membrane due to the clarity of the corneal tissue, and then place the instrument until it reaches where the fluid is, then gently press from one side to another.
se li aigue dessent maintenant, si voit li malaides devant lui et l’estrument en son oil.	If the water flows now, let the patient see before him and the instrument in his eye.
Aprés repose I petit, et se li aigue remonte la seconde voie, met la fuer avec l’estrument, et quant elle est ens fichie et ele ne monte, si estrai almagda legierement en tornoiant ta main poc et poc;	After resting for a little while, if the fluid rises again, apply pressure with the instrument, and when it is firmly inserted and the fluid no longer rises, then gently extract it in small rotations.
et puis remette en aigue un poc de seil gemme, et leive de ceu l’oil dedens.	and then add a little powdered ruby to the fluid, and lift the eye from it.
Puis met par defuer l’oil estoupes ou lainne moillie en oile roset et en abun d’uef, et lie avec l’oil sain.	Then place outside the eye plugs made of wool soaked in rose oil and an abundance of egg white, and tie them with a healthy eye.
Nos, et cil qui sont de nostre tens, mettons sus comin broiet avec abun d’uef.	We, and those of our time, apply it mixed with egg white in abundance.
Et se almagda n’i puet entrer en l’oil par sa duresce, car il i a de teilz homes qui ont trop durs les eulz, si covient que tu preignes l’estrument qui est apelez «alberit», de coi ci est li forme:	And if the almagda cannot enter the eye due to its hardness, for there are some people who have very hard eyes, then you must take the instrument called “alberit”, here is its form:
Et perce donques la conjunctive soulement, et n’aler mie trop em parfont, mais fai I leu subtil, puis i boute almagda, si com nos avons dit;	And then pierce only the conjunctiva, and do not go too deep, but make a delicate incision, then insert the instrument as we have said.
et au complissement de l’uevre appareille au malaide I dorteur avenant, en coi il dorme sus son dos en I leu tenebrous;	and at the completion of the work, prepare the patient for the doctor's arrival, in which he sleeps on his back in a dark place;
et soit deveez de toz movemens, et preigne legieres viandes, et ne mueve son chief ne a destre ne a senestre, et soit liiez selonc sa disposition jusc’a tier jor;	and let him be free of all movements, and give him light food, and do not move his head neither to the right nor left, and bind him according to his condition until the third day;
puis le deslie en cele maison meisme tenebrouse, et esprueve sa veue, et lou fai veoir aucunes choses, et puis li remet lou lien jusc’a septime jor;	then release him in the same dark house and test his vision, and show him some things, and then bind him again until the seventh day;
et ne covient mie que tu faices ceu en l’oure de la cure ou aprés l’incision maintenant, mais il covient que tu aliges ceu, por ceu que li aigue monte hastanment.	and it is not proper for you to do this during the time of treatment or immediately after the incision, but it is necessary to postpone this, because the fluid rises quickly.
se apostemes chaus vient, que tu desliies l’oil devant le septime jor, et l’adrece de ceu qui assouaige aposteme;	If an abscess forms, that you should not open the eye before the seventh day, and direct it as he who treats abscesses;
et quant il est apaisiez, si deslie la veue et met sus sa faice I orilliet por covrir aucun jor, et soit adés en celle maison tenebrouse.	and when it is healed, then open the eye and place a small piece of gold over it for several days, and let it be in a dark room.
Et puis isse de la maison poc et poc, et se convertisse en ses cas;	And then leave the house gradually, and return to his usual activities;
et saiches que nulz deciples ne se doit entremettre en cest cas.	and know that no student should interfere in this case.
Et uns vint a nos qui estoit de la Yrach, qui nos dist que en som pais faisoit om almagda perciet, a coi on succe l’aigue, mais toutevoie je n’en vis onques nul en nostre terre, ne je ne lou lis onques en livres des anciens;	And one came to us who was from the Irach, who told us that in his country they use small lancets to draw off fluid, but still I have never seen any such thing in our land, nor have I read about it in ancient books.
et par aventure c’est une novele chose.	And by chance it is a new thing.
Et ce sont les semblances des formes de almagda, por ceu que cil qui ne les conoit les voie;	And these are the appearances of the forms of almonds, so that those who do not recognize them see them;
et soient d’arain proprement:	and they should be properly of silver:
Et soient li chief d’aus de ceste meisme subtiliteit, et li derriene en III angles ague.	And let the front part of them be of the same subtlety, and the rear in three acute angles.
de la char sor le neis	of the flesh upon the nose
Aucune fois naissent ou neis chars ajostees diverses, de coi il i a aucunes qui semblent scorpions a mout de piez;	Sometimes the newly born creatures appear in various forms, some of which seem to have many legs like scorpions;
et si i a de telz ou il ait char enchancree de fuxe color, et si a char souef de bone color.	and there are some that have a body enlarged in red color, and below it has flesh of good color.
En celle donques de ces chars qui est souef, et ne mie enchancree, covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains encontre lou soleil;	In the case of those creatures that are below and not enlarged, you should have the patient sit between your hands facing the sun;
et oevre ses narines, et giete l’oncine a celles chars, et les trai fuers;	and work his nostrils, and throw the splint to those parts, and draw out the foreign object;
pues cope ceu que tu em pues sostenir au spatumile subtil agut d’une part, tant que tu saiches que celle char est toute ostee.	then hold it as you can sustain the sharp subtle spatum from one side until you know that the flesh is completely removed.
Et s’il en remaint aucune chose c’on ne puisse coper, si l’ovrez a tout I des estrumens subtil legierement, si qu’il n’i demoure rien;	And if there remains anything that cannot be cut, then treat it with all the subtle instruments gently, so that nothing remains.
et se sans te sormonte, ou aposteme chaus, si lou secort si com il covient;	and if it overflows from the abscess, then treat it as is appropriate;
et se c’est apostemes malignes, si te haste et lou cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez et soient ostees toutes les chars, puis giete ou neis aisil et aigue ou vin.	and if these are malignant abscesses, then hurry and cauterize until the blood is congealed and all the flesh is removed, then apply fresh and clean wine or vinegar to the nostrils.
Se li neis oevre, et moistors en vient jusc’a palais, saiches qu’il est sanez;	If the urine is being passed, and moisture reaches up to the palate, know that he is safe;
et se moistors ne perce si com il covient, saiches qu’il i a char nee en l’os desus, a coi li estrumens ne vient mie por taillier:	and if moisture does not reach as it should, know that there is flesh on the bone above, where the instrument cannot cut:
adonques covient il que tu i boutes I fil de lin un poc gros, et soit noez de mains nous, et ait entre chescun nout d’espaice I doit ou moins;	then you should insert a thick linen thread there, and tie it tightly by hand, with about an inch between each knot;
et mette li malaides lou chiés dou fil en son neif a som pooir, et traie en odorant tant qu’il viegne par lou neif dedens la bouche;	and place the patient's finger with the thread on his tooth as much as possible, and pull it gently until it comes through the tooth into the mouth;
et maintes fois font ensi li enfant as escoles, et c’est legiere chose a celui qui le vuet faire;	and often children at school do this, and it is an easy thing for one who wants to do it;
puis tien le chief qui vient par lou neif a une main, et l’autre chief qui vient par la bouche a l’autre main, et saiche l’un aprés l’autre en soiant as nous qui sont ou fil.	Then hold the end that comes from the neck in one hand, and the other end that comes from the mouth in the other hand, and pull them apart while noting us who are in the thread.
Fai ceu tant que tu saiches que li nout ont corrompue celle char, puis trai lou filz, essue le sanc, et moille lou fil en oignement egiptien, et le remet derechief au neis si com devant;	Do this until you see that the knots have corrupted the flesh, then pull out the thread, wipe away the blood, and moisten the thread in Egyptian ointment, and put it back into the nose as before;
fai ceu III jors ou plus, tant que li oignemens corrode tout ceu qui est demorez de char;	Do this for three days or more, until the ointment corrupts all that remains of the flesh;
et puis met ou neis une caine de plonc aucuns jors tant qu’il soit sanez, et s’il a mestier de medicines sechans, si en use;	and then place a bandage of lead on the nose for several days until it is healed, and if there is need for drying medications, use them;
et c’est li forme de l’estrument por purgier lou chief, a coi on distille les oiles et les medicines ou neis:	and this is the form of the instrument for purging the head, wherein one distills oils and medicines through it:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain, semblant a une lampe overte, si com une cainne, et li conduis ausi;	And whether it be of silver or copper, it resembles an open lamp, like a funnel, and the conduit is likewise;
et se tu vues, si fai une cainne close, et soit li estrumens plains por espurgier lou chief;	and if you prefer, make a closed funnel, and the instrument should be full for purging the head;
et ait I mainche au chief por lou tenir quant on chaufe l’oile ou aucune liquor.	and it should have a handle at the top to hold when heating the oil or any liquid.
de la char sor le neis	of the flesh upon the nose
Maintes fois naist au chief dou neis une maladie qui est apelee «telul», et croist et devient grans adés, tant qu’il est vis chose au regarder;	Many times a disease called "telul" arises on the head of the nose, and it grows and becomes large soon, so much so that it is visible to the eye;
et por ceu covient que tu lou copes au comencement, et l’oste tout fuer, puis met sor leu lou cautere ou la medicine ardant;	And for this reason, you must cut it at the beginning, remove all hair, then apply the cautery or the burning medicine.
et s’on le tarde a coper tant qu’il soit grans, si pren warde s’il est durs, de fuxe color, de povre sens:	And if you delay cutting it until it is large, be wary if it is hard, of a bad color, and lacking sensation:
si ne lou touchier mie de fer car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, car quant on le cope aucune fois, si en vient grant malice au malaide;	do not touch it with iron because it is an embedded abscess, for when you cut it even once, great harm comes to the patient;
