Quant li artere est route, et li cuir est soudez qui est sus, si en vient maintes fois apostemes, et tout aussi avient il a la voine enflee et aposteme;	When the artery is ruptured, and the skin above it is sealed, there often result abscesses; and likewise happens to a swollen vein and abscess;
et si le conoist on ensi quant c’est por l’artere, si est li apostemes lons em parfont;	and one recognizes this when it is due to the artery, as the abscesses are long and deep;
et quant tu le sens a tes dois, si sens I estraignement;	and when you feel it with your hands, you sense the tightness;
et quant c’est por la voine, si est reons defuer aparans;	and when it is due to the vein, it appears more superficially;
et c’est folie de coper cest aposteme, et meismement quant il est desoz les asseles et as angres et ou col et em mout d’autres leus, et est mout grans.	and it is foolish to incise this abscess, especially when it is located away from the axillae and angles and on the neck and in many other places, and it is very large.
Il covient donques eschuir la cure de fer, et celui qui est a chief covient eschuir ausi, et en celui qui est d’enfleure d’artere fent par desus le cuir dou lonc;	It is therefore necessary to avoid the iron treatment, and for him who has it at the head, one must also avoid it, and in the case of arterial swelling, make an incision above the skin.
puis oevre la taille as oncines, et depart bellement l’artere des toiles, tant qu’ele soit descoverte;	then work the area with scissors, and carefully separate the artery from the surrounding tissue, until it is exposed;
puis boute desoz li une aguille, et la fai percier jusc’a l’autre costeit, et estraint l’artere d’un fil double en II leus, selonc ceu que je t’ai ensigniet en l’estraction des II arteres qui sont en temples;	then insert a needle on one side and pierce it to the other side, and tie off the artery with a doubled thread in two places, as I have taught you in extracting the two arteries that are in the temples;
puis point le leu qui est entre les II liens d’un intromissoire tant que li sans en isse qui i est, et soit deliiez li aposteme;	then puncture the area between the two ligatures with an instrument so that the blood flows out which is there, and release the abscess;
puis amenistre la cure que enjanre bowe, tant que li liien chient;	Then administer the treatment that induces vomit, until the patient relieves.
puis cure ceu d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then treat them with appropriate ointment until they are healed.
et se li apostemes est por la taille de la voinne, si covient que tu teignes a ta main ceu que tu pues de l’aposteme a tout le cuir, puis boute l’aguille desoz le leu que tu tiens a ta main, et la fai percier, et i ait I fil double, si que tu le trais de l’autre costeit;	And if the abscess is near a vein, you should mark with your hand the area of the abscess on the skin, then insert the needle under the spot you are holding, and pierce it, and place double thread there so that you can draw it from the other side.
puis lie l’aposteme, si com je t’ai dit, ou liien de l’une de II pars as II chiés dou fil;	Then ligature the abscess as I told you, using one part of the thread around each of the two threads.
et se tu doutes que li filz n’isse fuer, si i reboute une autre aguille a tout I fil desoz tout l’aposteme a l’incision de la premiere aguille, et estraint les filz en IIII leus;	And if you fear that the thread might come loose, insert another needle along the entire length of the first incision through the abscess, and tie the threads in four places.
puis cope l’aposteme tant que li superfluitez en isse, puis cope la superfluiteit dou keur et laisse ceu qui est liiez;	Then incise the abscess until the excess matter comes out, then incise the excess matter from the heart and leave what is bound;
puis met sus I drapeil moilliet en vin et en oile, puis li amenistre cures de tentes et d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then place a damp cloth on it with wine and oil, then treat it with bandages and ointments until he is well.
des apostemes des ners	abscesses of the nerves
Ausi com aposteme vienent en l’artere et en la voine, vienent aposteme as ners quant il sont ferut, ou par trop grant travail, et semblans choses.	Just as abscesses occur in the artery and vein, abscesses also affect the nerves when they are injured, or from excessive labor, and similar things.
Et ceu avient plus sovent as adjutoires et as dois et en toz leus ou il ait jointures, et c’est I grief apostemes, et sa color semble la color dou cors, et est em plusors dispositions sens dolor;	And this happens more often in the shoulders and elbows and in all places where there are joints, and these are severe abscesses, and its color resembles the color of the skin, and it is painful in various conditions.
et quant on l’estraint forment, si sent li malaides dolor, et n’est mie em parfont dou cors, mais desoz lou keur;	and when it is pressed hard, the patient feels pain, and it is not in the flesh deeply, but near the heart;
et muet bien de toutes pars, et ne va ne avant ne arrier, ne desoz ne desus, et celui qui est en jointures ne covient mie coper par fer:	And it moves well on all sides, neither forward nor backward, nor sideways nor upwards, and the one who is in joints should not be cut with iron:
par aventure i vanroit contraction;	by chance there would be contraction;
et cil qui est ou chief ou ou front, fent le cuir au spatumile.	and for the one who is in the head or forehead, cut the skin with a spatula.
Se li apostemes est petis, si le tien a unes tenailles, et le cope en sa racine;	If the abscess is small, hold it with forceps and cut it at its root;
et s’il est grans, si le sospent a l’oncine, et l’escorche, puis l’oste et assemble la plaie a la costure, et lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and if it is large, suspend it with an ounce of material, and peel it, then remove it and stitch the wound together, and treat it until it heals.
des grosses boces pendans	large hanging pouches
Aucune fois avient en ventres et ne mie autre part thelul, et est une maladie qui est apelee «funge» par la semblance d’aus, et est li racine subtilz, et li chiez gros;	Sometimes it occurs in bellies and not elsewhere, and it is a disease called "fungus" by its resemblance to such things, and the root is subtle, and the mass is large;
et en i a de petis et de mout grans;	and there are both small and very large ones;
et je vis I home qui en avoit II ou ventre qui estoient plus semblans a funges que ai autre chose, et n’i avoit point de difference, et estoient blanc, et avoient menue racine, et estoient jai fendut, et en corroit adés moistor.	and I saw a man who had two of them in his belly which were more similar to fungi than anything else, and there was no difference between them, they were white, and had fine roots, and were slightly split, and moisture corroded them quickly.
Je les copai et trovai en l’un XVIII onces pesant, et en l’autre VI З., et li ovraiges en l’incision si est que tu regardes se li malaides est moistes, et li color de l’artelul est blainche et moiste et de subtil racine;	I removed them and found one weighing eighteen ounces, and the other six. The procedure for incising is such that you check if the patient is moist, and the color of the tissue is white and moist with a fine root;
si le cope au spatumile large, et soient en ta presence li cautere au feu.	cut it with a spatula wide, and have the fire cautery ready in your presence.
Car au taillier vient maintes fois trop grans decorremens de sanc, et se li sans te vaint, si te haste donques dou cauterizer;	For in cutting there often come too great flows of blood, and if the blood overwhelms you, then hasten to use the cautery;
et se tu vois le malaide espoanteit et paourous de l’incision dou fer, si prent I fil de plonc bien fait, et en lie l’artelul si com nos avons dit, et le laisse II jors;	and if you see the patient frightened and fearful of the iron incision, then take a well-made linen thread, and tie it around the joint as we have said, and leave it for two days;
et puis le restraint, et ne cesser d’estraindre lou fil de plonc tant qu’il cope l’artelul, et chiece par lui sens travail;	and then restrain it, and do not stop restraining the linen thread until it fits the joint properly, and work with it carefully;
et se les racines sont grosses, si a paour au coper meismement por le ventre, mais tu em pues bien coper la moitiet, puis le cauterize qu’il ne reviegne;	and if the roots are thick, be careful when cutting to avoid injuring the abdomen, but you may cut half of it, then cautery it so that it does not regrow;
puis cure la plaie, et garde que tu ne coper le thelul qui est de fuxe color et de povre sens et de lait regart.	Then treat the wound, and be careful not to cut the tendon which is of pink color and poor sensation and milk-white appearance.
Car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, et je venrai a la cure de chancre ci aprés.	For this is an embedded abscess, and I will come to the treatment of the ulcer shortly.
quant li boude ist fuer	when the swelling is strong
Se li apparance de la boude vient par cautere de plaie ou de fendure de syfac, et est sus le ventre et en ist aucuns des bouez, si com il avient en autres routures, ou de sanc qui cort de voines ou d’arteres selonc ceu qui est devant, ou de ventositeit;	If the appearance of swelling comes from a cautery on a wound or tear on the surface, and it is on the belly and some of the bowels are involved, as happens in other ruptures, or from blood that flows from veins or arteries according to what is before mentioned, or from windiness;
et se c’est par la routure dou syfac et par l’issue dou bouel, si est li color de l’aposteme semblans a la color dou cors, et est legiere chose sens dolor, et apert de diverse issue.	and if this is due to the rupture of the surface and the exit of the bowels, then the color of the abscess resembles the color of the skin, and it causes little pain, and is clear from various exits.
Et se c’est por l’issue de l’intestine, adonques est il plus divers, et quant on le presse a ses dois si se repont, et puis revient, et par aventure si est sarrez, et agrandist mout a l’entree dou bain et por fort travail.	And if it is due to an issue from the intestine, then it is more diverse, and when one presses on both sides, it responds and then returns, and perhaps it is constricted, and greatly enlarges at the entrance of the bath and for hard labor.
Et se c’est por moistor, c’est legiere chose, et apert bien quant tu le presses a ta main, ne ne constraint mie;	And if it is due to moisture, it is a minor issue, and becomes clear when you press it with your hand, without any restriction;
et se c’est por sanc, si apert par ces signes li apostemes gros et dur, et est fichiez selonc une quantiteit;	And if it is due to blood, then these signs clearly indicate large and hard abscesses, and they are fixed according to a certain quantity;
et se c’est por ventositeit, si est souef au tochier, et li ovraiges si est que tu regarde se li apparance est por le sanc de l’artere, ou de la voine, ou ventositeit.	And if it is due to windiness, then it is shallow to touch, and the treatment is that you observe whether the appearance is due to arterial blood, or from a vein, or windiness.
Si covient que tu laisses la cure.	It is necessary that you leave the treatment.
Car il en a doutance et paor, si com je t’ai dit ou chapistre des apostemes, por l’artere et por la voine.	For there is doubt and fear about it, as I told you in the chapter on abscesses, concerning the artery and the vein.
Et se li apparance est por l’intestine ou lou boueil, si covient que tu comandes au malaide qu’il teigne son alaine, et soit estendus tout drois, puis seigne d’enche tout entor la boude;	And if the appearance is due to the intestines or the bile, then you must instruct the patient to hold their breath, and lie completely straight, then incise all around the wound;
puis le comande a gesir sovin entre tes mains, puis va entor le leu que tu as signiet a tout le spatumile, puis estent la moitiet de l’aposteme au desus a tout le grant uncine;	then instruct the patient to lie still between your hands, then go around the place you marked with the spatula, then extend half of the abscess above with the large forceps;
puis le lie entor d’un fil fort, ou d’une corde de fort soie fermement, et soit li nous dou liien assolz;	Then bind the area tightly with a strong thread or a rope of thick silk, and ensure that the bandage is firmly in place;
puis oevre la moitiet de l’aposteme estendut sus le liien, et i boute ton doit indice, et quier l’intestine;	Then work on half of the abscess extended over the bandage, and place your index finger inside to seek the intestine;
se tu le trueves pris dou liien, si le deslie, et boute l’intestine au defuer dou ventre;	if you find it caught in the bandage, then loosen it, and push the intestine back into the abdomen;
et se tu trueves le boueil, si le prent a l’oncine, et en cope la superfluiteit;	and if you find the bowel, grasp it with your hook and cut away the excess;
et se li artere te fait contraire, ou li voine, si vai belement entor, puis revien a ton ovraige et pren II aguilles, et i boute II fors filz, et boute les II aguilles entor ceu que tu as fait en crois que tu feis percier;	and if the artery or vein obstructs you, proceed carefully around them, then return to your work and take two needles, and insert two strands of thread outside what you have done in a cross shape to ensure puncturing;
puis estrain l’aposteme en IIII leus sus les aguilles, et se tu vues, oste les aguilles, et laisse lou leu tant qu’il porrisse, et chiece li char morte par soi;	Then incise the abscess in four places over the needles, and if you wish, remove the needles, and leave the wound to pus until it necroses, and the dead tissue falls out on its own.
ou tu la cope quant elle iert subtiliie et porrie, puis le cure de ceu qu’il covient, et cheve l’aposteme si com nos avons dit;	When you cut it when it is subtle and pus-filled, then treat it as needed, and drain the abscess as we have said.
et estrai le sanc ou la moistor que tu trueves, puis cure le leu de ceu qu’il couvient, et soude le leu.	And extract the blood or moisture that you find, then treat the wound as needed, and close the wound.
dou chancre	of the ulcer
Nos avons dit en la division les semblances de chancre, et coment on i doit ovrer par medicines, et coment on doit eschuer la cure de fer;	We have discussed in the section the similarities of ulcers, and how one should treat them with medicine, and how to avoid treatment with iron.
et disons le chancre enjanreit en la marris, et grant cautele a en la cure, et dirent li ancien que quant chancres est en leu ou on le puet raier si com chancre qui est em mameles, et en la cuixe, et en semblans leus, et le doit tout oster quant il est en l’encomencement;	And we say the ulcer spreads to the marrow, and great care is needed in its treatment, and the ancients said that when ulcers are in places where they can be scraped out such as an ulcer on a breast or thigh, and in similar places, it should all be removed at the beginning.
et quant il est grans et anciens, si ne covient mie que tu l’aproches, car je n’en poi onques nul saner;	And when it is large and old, you should not approach it, for I have never seen anyone heal such.
ne nulz n’en sana onques devant moi.	nor has anyone ever been healed before me.
Et li ovraiges, quant il est en leu ou on le puet oster, si com nos avons dit, est que tu purge aucune fois le malaide de cole noire;	And in the places where it can be removed, as we have said, it is that you should sometimes purge the patient of black bile;
puis le fai sainier s’il ait manifeste repletion, puis afaite le malaide I boin leu por faire l’ovraige;	Then make it bleed if there is obvious fullness, then position the patient properly to perform the work;
puis giete tes oncines ou chancre, et le cheve de toutes pars, et l’oste de toutes pars sens rien laissier;	Then apply your poultices to the ulcer, and remove hair from all parts, and remove tissue from all parts leaving nothing behind;
et laisse corre le sanc tout fuer, et espreint bien le leu a ta main ou a aucune chose, et se li decorremens de sanc te fait contraire de l’incision de l’artere ou de la voine, si le cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	and let the blood flow completely, and mark well the place with your hand or some object, and if the outflow of blood is contrary to the incision of an artery or vein, then cauterize until the bleeding stops;
puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it further until it is healed.
de ydropisie	of hydropsy
Nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’idropisie, et en queil maniere li assemblee de l’aigue est faite, et les signes de chescune semblance, et la cure qui est faite par medicines, et cele qui est curee par fer:	We have already described in the division the similarities of dropsy, and how the accumulation of fluid is formed, and the signs of each condition, and the treatment done with medicine, and that which is treated with iron:
si est eclites soulement;	It is swollen only;
et ne doit on touchier de fer en ces II semblances:	and one should not touch with iron in these two similar cases:
c’est a savoir, tympanites et yposarche, car c’est mortelz chose;	that is to say, tympany and ileus, for it is a fatal thing;
donques quant tu medicines ceste semblance de ydropisie qui est apelee «eclites» de medicines, et li cure ne profite, si regarde se li malaides est foibles, ou s’il ait autre maladie que ydropisie, si com toust et solution de ventre et semblans choses;	then when you treat this case of dropsy which is called "swelling" with medicines, and the cure does not help, look to see if the patient is weak, or if he has another disease besides dropsy, such as colds and loose bowels and similar things;
si n’i touchier de fer, car il i a doutance;	do not use iron in this case, for there is doubt;
et se tu vois le malaide de fort vertut, et il n’a autre maladie que ydropisie soulement, et il n’est mie trop jones ne trop vielz, si dois ensi ovrer:	and if you see the patient is of strong temperament, and he has no other disease but dropsy only, and he is neither too young nor too old, then you should act thus:
lieve le malaide droit sus tes mains, et li ministres presse le ventre em boutant l’aigue a la plus basse partie dou pis, puis pren le spatumile espinous selonc ceste forme:	Lay the patient straight on your hands, and have the minister press the belly by inserting water into the lowest part of the abdomen, then take the spatula according to this form:
Et soit trenchans de II pars.	And let there be cutting from two sides.
a pointe, et toutevoie ne soit mie si entrans qu’il puist venir jusc’a l’intestine quant on le fiche ens, et ne le puist blecier;	point it, and ensure that it does not enter so deeply as to reach the intestine when inserted, and cannot be withdrawn;
puis regarde se li ydropisie est enjanree devers les intestines:	then check if the edema is located towards the intestines:
si covient que tu fendes ensus de la boude III dois droit desoz sus lou poignil;	if necessary, you should cut above the navel three fingers wide on each side of the belly;
et se li ydropisie est por la maladie dou foie, si soit ta fendure au senestre de la boude III dois;	and if the edema is due to liver disease, then your incision should be on the left side of the navel three fingers wide;
et se c’est por la miuce, si soit a destre, et ne covient mie que li malaides gise sus la fendure que les superfluitez ne corrent a celui foible leu;	and if it is for the midsection, let it be to the right, and it must not be that the patient lies over the crease so that the excesses do not flow to the weaker area;
puis perce tout le cuir a l’estrument, et le boute, et lieve ta main a tout le spatumile entre le cuir et le syfac ausi com en escorchant a la quantiteit d’une ungle ou enqui entor;	then pierce the skin with the instrument, and cut it, and lift your hand to scrape off all the suppurative material between the skin and the tissue as you would in flaying, about the thickness of a nail or slightly more;
puis perce lou syfac tant que li spatumile viegne au leu vuit, et c’est li leus de l’aigue, puis le trai fuer, et i boute cest estrument de coi ci est li forme:	then puncture the tissue until the pus comes to an open place, which is where the fluid will drain, then draw it out with force, and use this instrument whose form is as follows:
Et est semblans a une caine d’argent subtil, et est d’arain ou d’archaut legier, et a en la partie desoz I petit pertus;	And it is similar to a thin silver chain, and it is made of light iron or reed, and has small holes in one part;
et ou costeit d’une part, III pertus;	and when there is a cost (rib) on one side, three perforations;
et II d’autre part, et I d’autre;	and two on the other side, and one on another;
et est li chiés tailliez si com une penne, et c’est li forme de l’incision dont li escrivains taille la penne:	and the head is cut like a feather, and this is the shape of the incision that writers make on a quill:
au chief desus est li alemele, si que quant li estrumens vient a l’aigue, si dessent maintenant sus l’estrument;	at the top is the blade, so that when the instrument comes to the tip, it now descends along the instrument;
vuide la donques la moitiet ou la tierce part, car se tu en vuides plus qu’il ne covient en celle houre, par aventure si muert li malaides por la resolution de son esperit de l’arme, ou il chiet paumez, ou il aproche a la mort;	empty then half or one-third of it, for if you empty more than is necessary at that hour, by chance the patient may die from the resolution of his spirit due to the weapon, or he falls fainting, or he approaches death;
mais en vuide selonc la quantiteit de sa vertut, et selonc ceu que les dispositions de la vertut dou malaide signifient, et ses poulz;	but according to the emptiness according to the quantity of its virtue, and according to what the conditions of the virtue of the patient signify, and his pulse;
puis trai l’estrument et retien l’aigue, et elle est retenue maintenant por le keur qui estoupe le pertus qui est sus le syfac, de coi j’ai parleit, que tu perces selonc ceste maniere;	then draw the instrument and retain the fluid, and it is now retained for the heart which stops up the passage that is above the diaphragm, of which I have spoken, that you pierce according to this manner;
puis rencomence l’estrument l’autre jor, se tu vois le malaide soffrant ceu, et trai de l’aigue une petite quantiteit;	then restart the instrument on the other day, if you see the patient suffering from this, and draw off a small quantity of fluid;
fai ce aucun jor, et te garde de foloier tant qu’il ni demore mais c’un poc d’aigue.	do this on some days, and be careful not to overdo it so that no more than a little bit of fluid remains.
Et se tu doutes sus le malaide, et tu i lais mout d’aigue, si le cure de la sepulture ou sablon chaut, et par mout sueir ou bain et au soleil, et se teigne de boivre;	And if you are uncertain about the patient, leave them much in water, and treat with the cure of the grave or hot sand, and by much sweating or bathing and in the sun, and dye from drinking;
et le cure de medicines desiccatives tant qu’il soit sanez, et cauterize sus l’estomac et sus lou foie et sus l’esplen aprés l’estraction de l’aigue, si com j’ai dit devant.	and treat with drying medicines until he is healthy, and cauterize on the stomach and liver and spleen after the extraction of water, as I said before.
de l’estopement de la verge	about the impediment of the penis
Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n’ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n’est mie en son leu.	Sometimes children are born who have no opening in the penis, or the opening is small, or it is not in its proper place.
Si le covient tantost qu’il n’aist percier a tout I spatumile molt subtil selonc ceste forme:	It is necessary to pierce it immediately throughout the spatumile very finely according to this form:
puis met ou pertus I clo subtil de plonc, et le lie et le tien ensi III jors ou IIII et quant il vuet faire urine, si soit ostez li clos, et faice urine, et puis li remet;	then put a fine plug of lint in the opening, and tie it securely for three days or four, and when he wants to urinate, remove the plug, let him urinate, and then replace it;
et par aventure nen i couvient point, car li urine qui vient fuer ne lou laisse close.	and perhaps it is not necessary, for the urine that comes from above does not leave it closed.
Cil de cui li pertus est petis, si est medicinez dou clo de plonc, si com nos avons dit, si s’eslargera.	He whose opening is small, if treated with the cloth of flax as we have said, will be enlarged.
Cil qui n’ont mie le pertus en lor leu sont bleciet, car aucun naissent qui ont le pertus au chief de la verge, por coi il ne puient pissier avant s’il ne lievent lor verge en haut;	Those who do not have the urethral opening in its proper place are afflicted, for some are born with it at the head of the penis, so they cannot urinate unless they lift their penis upwards.
et ne pueent enjanrer por ceu que li matiere ne puet venir jusc’a la marris, et c’est une male maladie.	and they cannot urinate because the matter cannot reach the bladder, and this is a serious illness.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos, puies estent le chief de la verge et le cope ausi com la taille d’une penne, si ke li pertus chiece em mileu, si com il covient;	And the method is that the patient lies supine on their back, then stretches the head of the penis and holds it as thick as a quill, so that the urethral opening points straight ahead, as it should.
et te garde de decorrement de sanc qui i vient maintes fois, et s’il avient, si l’estainche de ceu qui estainche sanc, et cure la plaie tant qu’il soit sanez.	and be cautious of bleeding that often occurs, and if it happens, stop the bleeding as one would for any bleed, and treat the wound until it is healed.
des pustules de la verge	pustules of the shaft
Maintes fois vienent cist albathe en la verge, et est une apparance de char laide;	Often this swelling comes in the penis, and it is an ugly appearance of flesh;
et en i a malignes et non malignes;	and there are both malignant and non-malignant ones;
si covient que tu les preignes a I oncine subtil, et les cope et munde toutes, puis met sus coton moilliet en oignement egiptien;	you should take them out with a fine needle, and cut and clean all of them, then put on moistened cotton with Egyptian ointment;
puis le cure d’oignement diafinicon tant qu’il soit sanez.	then cure it with Diafinicon ointment until it is healed.
Et se li albathe est maligne, de pute color et depuant, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere.	And if the wound is malignant, of a foul color and putrid, then you must apply cauterization to it.
Quant tu l’as copeit, et se li albathe est en som la verge, et en ait partie dedens la peil et partie defuer, si covient que tu oste l’albathe qui est dedens premier;	When you have cut it, and if the swelling is in the shaft of the penis, and part of it is inside the skin and part outside, then you must remove the part that is inside first;
et quant il est soudez, si le cure defuer.	And when it is sealed, then treat it to avoid.
Car quant tu le cures ensamble, si n’est mie asseurez li chiez de la verge qu’il ne soit perciez, et vient noiror et corruption en son la verge et ou coion;	For when you treat it together, the head of the penis is not assured that it will not be pierced, and blackness and corruption come to the penis and the testicles;
si covient chever tout ceu qui est noir et corrumput, puis lie sus l’emplaustre de miel et de farine qui soit fait d’escorce de poumes grenates et de veces, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	It is necessary to remove all that is black and corrupted, then apply a plaster made of pomegranate peel and vinegar, then treat it with other treatments until it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si amenistre le cautere lunaire selonc ceste forme:	And if bleeding occurs, then treat with a lunar cauterization according to this form:
Li cauteres si aide as II dispositions ensamble:	The cauterization helps with both conditions together:
c’est asavoir, au decorrement de sanc, et a la corruption;	that is to say, in the discharge of blood, and in corruption;
et se li chiés de la verge est corrumpus et retrais, si covient que tu boutes ou conduit de la verge une cainne de plonc, et pisse li malaides parmi;	and if the head of the penis is corrupted and retracted, it is necessary to insert a silver tube into the urethra, and the patient should urinate through it;
et quant li pelz iert aerse au chief de la verge qui avient a ces qui n’ont mie esteit circoncis, ou il avient por plaie ou por aposteme, si covient donques que tu l’escorches a I estrument cheveit, tant que li liiens soit desliiez, et soit delivrez li chiez de la verge de toutes pars;	And when the hairs are raised at the head of the penis which happens to those who have not been circumcised, and it becomes an injury or an abscess, then you must burn it with a sharp instrument until the band is loosened, and release the head of the penis from all sides;
et se c’est grief chose de deviser ceu, si covient que tu l’escorches a I spatumile aucun poc dou chief de la verge et de la peil;	And if it is difficult to discuss this matter, then you must burn with the cautery slightly at the head of the penis and on the skin;
puis dessevre belement entre II, et i met I subtil drapeil de lin moilliet an aigue froide, qu’il n’aerse derechief.	Then carefully separate them, and place a fine linen cloth soaked in cold water on it so that it does not raise again.
de la circoncision	of circumcision
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies;	Circumcision is not like the separation of other wounds;
toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.	Though we perform this work of our will, and properly for children, it is necessary that we do the best work, and the lightest for salvation.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	I say that the ancients did not speak of circumcision for their children, as they did not practice it in their law, and we only have what we have acquired through experience.
Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor I dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule;	For I have seen the majority of masters and seniors who performed circumcisions around the age of one year, and for those with strong constitutions, and for all newborns;
si fuioit li keurs car il i a II toiles, et par aventure si cope on celi desus et demore celle desoz.	It is dangerous because there are two layers, and by chance one cuts through the upper layer and leaves the lower;
Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n’est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre;	Now there is the need to cut again, and the pain is doubled, and for the purification which is at one year old, the tip of the member is not assured;
et a la mundification de l’ungle par aventure eschaipe li fer, et corront l’uevre, et maintes fois naissent ensi qu’il n’ont mestier de mundification et je l’ai veut.	and in the purification of the nail, by chance the iron slips, and ruins the work, and many times they are born such that they do not need purification, and I have seen it.
De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le liien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l’experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.	From the healing that is done with threads throughout the entire limb, I have discovered the goodness of the experiment, for the threads cut precisely both above and below.
Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en I tout soul tens;	For when you press your hand, cut evenly in one continuous motion;
mais que li filz soit bien estrois entor lou cuir;	but the thread should be tightly wrapped around the skin;
et soit li maniere dou premier ovraige si est que tu faices penser l’enfant, s’il entent, que tu ne li fais fuer que liier le fil entor la verge tant soulement, et pues le fai esjoir en toutes les manieres que tu pues;	and the method of the first procedure is such that you should make the child, if he understands, believe that you are only tying the thread around his member and then you can amuse him in any way you can;
puis le fai ester entre tes mains tout droit, et repont les forces entre tes mains ou desoz tes piez que li enfes ne les voie, ne aucun des estrumens;	then hold him straight between your hands, and place the instruments between your hands or behind your feet so that the child does not see them, nor any of the instruments;
puis boute ta main a la verge et souffle ou keur, et la trai en haut tant que li chiés de la verge soit ens;	then place your hand on the member and blow at its root, and pull it up until the head of the member is engaged;
puis la mundifie bien de l’ordure qui i est assemblee, puis lie le leu signiet d’un fil double, puis la lie desoz I poc a I autre liien;	Then clean well of the dirt that is assembled there, then bind the place with a double thread, then bind from one pit to another ligature;
et la tien as II dois par la seconde lieeure au pouchet et au doit indice, et cope entre les II liiens, puis lieve le keur desus hastanment et trai le chief de la verge;	and hold it with two fingers by the second binding at the pouch and at the right index, and cut between the two ligatures, then lift the heart quickly and pull the head of the rod;
puis laisse corre le sanc poc et poc, car c’est li muedres;	then let the blood flow drop by drop, for this is the safer method;
et met poudre sus et sus la poudre I drapeil glueit d’un moieuf d’uef cuit destempreit d’aigue rose, confit avec oile roset boin et fres, et lou laisse sus jusc’a l’autre jor, et le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and put powder on and above the powder place a piece of cloth glued with one yolk of cooked egg diluted with rose water, prepared with good and fresh oil of roses, and leave it there until the next day, and treat it again as needed until it is healed.
Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste:	The form of the forces for purification is thus:
li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	the two heads should be sharp and should be as large as the shaft equally:
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision;	the mistake in purification is when the pus inside goes to the incision;
donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme;	then you must extend it to your fingernail, just as the pus forms an abscess;
et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	and cut it equally, and if you cannot hold it to your fingernail, then hold it with forceps, and then cut it.
Et s’il trespassent III jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement;	And if they transgress for three days, and that which is below the thigh swells, then leave it until the abscess is sufficiently healed, and lightly scrape it;
si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.	Move the part as much as you can, and avoid the shaft of the penis, so that it is not harmed.
Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point;	Treat the wound with powders that we have discussed in the chapter on powders, and if you cut into the heart too deeply, and it goes beyond what is necessary, it will do no harm;
cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	treat it as we have said until it is healed.
dou retenement de l’urine	from the retention of urine
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division;	The retention of urine is due to the obstruction of stones, or clotted blood, or bile, or dead tissue, or similar things, as we have said in the section;
et se li urine n’est desliie , et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz;	and if the urine is not released, and you see that the retention is due to a stone that is in the neck of the bladder, then it is necessary for the patient to be bent over their knees;
et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet;	and place the feet on the back, and extend the stomach from above the back, and have the patient pull in their abdomen as much as they can;
et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e;	and then the necks of the bladder are constrained to express the stone above, so that the urine is loosened and;
et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme:	and if it does not come, as we have said, and the patient feels great pain, then you must administer extraction with all the instrument called "syringe", of which here is the form:
et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil;	and let it be of fine silver, thin and drawn out, like the feather of a bird;
et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	and let the tube be one palm in length and a half, and let it be fine at the tip.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren I fil double, et lie au chief I poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue;	And the method of urine evacuation is such that you take a doubled thread, tie one end to a piece of wool or cotton, and put the other end of the thread into the urethra;
et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus I siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede;	and trim the excess wool and push it up to the end of the thread, then grease the urethra with oil or butter and egg yolk, and have the patient sit on a chair, and massage the bladder and penis with warm olive oil and vinegar;
puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude;	Then gently insert the syringe into the vein until it reaches the root of the vein, then fold the vein above toward the bulb;
puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors;	Then push the syringe forward until it reaches the bladder, and feel the patient’s sensation come up to the empty space, but this is not done according to this order unless the path it follows is twisted;
puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine;	Then stretch the thread through all the wool bit by bit, and the urine follows the wool, then pull it out, and let the urine flow;
et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	and continue with the syringe until the bladder is empty, and the patient feels relieved.
des maladies de la vessie	diseases of the bladder
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When pus or blood comes to the bladder, and putrefaction is gathered there, and you wish to introduce liquids and medicines, use all the instruments which are called "clepsydre", and this is its form:
Elle est close, et si a III pertus:	It is closed, and has three openings:
II d’une part, et I d’autre, si com tu vois;	II from one side, and I from the other, as you see;
et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est;	and the hair of the place where the medicine is applied should be such that it closes off the opening well so that one cannot draw out moisture, and insert when necessary;
et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens;	and when you wish to apply your medicines to the bladder, place the head of the catheter in the moisture, and draw it out with the extractor that is inside;
si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens;	you will draw out the moisture with the catheter, and then firmly press the extractor inside;
si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira;	the moisture will enter inside, and it will now reach the bladder, so that the patient can feel it;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie:	and this is the form of the subtle enema with which one administers to the bladder:
si est ci:	this is it:
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut;	It is made of silver or reed, and the tip is higher;
et desoz a I sein ou li liiens chiet;	and direct it toward the side where the ligament falls;
puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les II seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe I poc celle moistor sus le feu;	then take a sheep's bladder and put in the liquid with which you wish to administer the enema, then tie it between the two sides securely with a strong double thread, and heat the pot of that liquid over the fire;
puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie;	then insert the tip of the enema into the penis, then squeeze your hand along the bladder to push all the liquid gradually until the patient feels that the liquid has reached the bladder;
et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai I cercle, et le perce rondement entor;	And if you do not have a bladder, take a piece of parchment, make a circle out of it, and pierce it roundly around;
puis boute I fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble I dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument;	then thread a strong wire through these holes, then join the circle as one joins a sieve, and place within it what you wish of oil and moisture and water, and attach it to the instrument;
et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	and do as you did with the bladder, pressing with your hand until the moisture comes to the bladder.
de la piere	of the stone
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines;	We have already mentioned in the section the methods of stones and their extraction along with medicines;
et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille;	and I have said the difference between the stone formed in the kidneys, and all the signs, and which stones one should operate to remove;
et en la vessie, et en la verge;	and in the bladder, and in the penis;
et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	and I will tell you clearly and briefly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit;	I say that the stone which is formed in the bladder happens more often to children, and this is a sign that the urine skips from the bladder, similar to acute conditions in its subtlety;
et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist;	and he clearly sees urine, and the patient scratches his penis, and does so many times, and then becomes dizzy;
et a mout de ces saut li fondemens;	and in many of these cases, the foundations are weak;
et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont IIII ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece;	and the healing of children is easy until they are four years old, and it is very difficult in the elderly, and for adults it is moderate, for those who are between young adulthood and old age;
et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	And the treatment is easier for those who have large stones than for those who have small ones.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.	And when we come to the treatment, it is necessary first to clean the patient with an enema, to draw out all the feces that are in the intestines.
Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	For it sometimes hinders in seeking the stone.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut;	Then take the patient by the feet, and raise him up and move towards his back, so that the stone descends to the bottom of the bladder, and it sometimes comes out from a higher place;
puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval;	then have him sit between your hands which are prepared, and his hands should be behind his thighs, so that the bladder is completely inclined downward;
puis la quier et la touche dedens;	then press and feel inside;
se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.	if you feel the stone in its place, then hurry now to cut into the stone.
Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis;	And if it does not fall to the touch of everything, moisten your middle finger with oil from your left hand, if the patient is female, or your thumb, if the patient is a fully grown male;
et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie;	and insert it into its fundament, and search for the stone, and when you feel it with your finger, draw it to the bladder neck;
puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	then press with your finger, and remove the stone where you wish to cut.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille;	And instruct the assistant to press the bladder with his hand, and tell him to spread his right hand over the genitals upwards, and with his left hand remove the skin which is below the genitals in the area where the incision will be made;
puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	Then place the spatula over it, which is its form:
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre;	And make an incision between the genitals and the anus, not in the middle but on the left side of the navel;
et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans;	and it should be straight over the stone, and your two hands should immediately be at the anus, and the incision should be wide enough on the outside, and inside narrow according to the size of the stone, not too large;
par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail;	by chance the pressure may cause your hand at the anus to jump outward without effort;
et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges:	and know that there may be stones with corners and edges:
si est griés a issir;	It is painful to exit;
et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	and it is like one who is swollen, similar to a flower bud, and round, with a slight opening.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant;	For those who have corners and edges, make the size larger;
et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe;	and if it does not jump out, then you must clamp with pliers that are like a file at the top to firmly hold the stone so that it does not escape;
ou tu boute desoz li I estrument subtil corbé au chief;	where you insert from the side a delicate curved instrument at the top;
et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge I poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole;	and if you cannot manage it this way, then enlarge the opening slightly, and if blood flows out, clamp it with vitriol;
et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors.	And if there is more than one stone, place the largest first at the neck of the bladder, then cut above it, then draw it out forcefully, and the smaller ones after if there are several.
Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.	And if it is very large, you must wait and make a larger incision.
Car II choses avienent au malaide:	For two things happen to the patient:
ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder;	either he dies, or urine comes immediately preventing the wound from closing;
mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces;	but still, strive to extract it, or use pliers to remove it piece by piece;
et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus I drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut;	and when you have completed your work, apply the wound with incense and aloes and dragon's blood, and bind it tightly, then place a damp cloth over it in oil and wine, or in oil and rose water and cold water, to soothe the hot abscess;
puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	Then place the patient on their neck, and do not loosen the bandage until the third day.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you dislocate it, thoroughly wash the area well with oil and water, then treat it with diafinicon ointment and basilicon ointment until it is healed.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine:	And if abscesses and infections come into the wound and blood coagulates in the bladder, causing retention of urine, which is known to occur in such a manner that it clots along with the urine:
boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit;	Insert your finger into the wound, and extract that blood, for if it remains there, it will corrupt the bladder, and cause harm.
puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then clean the wound with water and herbs and bind it, and assist in all ways you know until he is healed;
et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les II cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	and it is necessary that every time you treat him, you bind both thighs, and apply the medications to the affected area.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir;	And if the stone is small, and it is in the urethra passage, stuck inside, and the urine cannot exit;
si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.	if he treats it as I say, you should cut it multiple times, and he is excused from the cutting due to this treatment.
Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	I have already tested this in this way.
Pren I foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a III angles fichiees en I tison:	Take an iron fork according to this form and let it have three prongs fixed in one handle:
puis pren I fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie;	then take some thread and tie it around the penis below the stone, so that it cannot move back into the bladder;
puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere;	then insert the probe gently into the penis until it reaches the stone;
et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part;	and rotate the probe with your hand against the stone bit by bit, until you can pierce the stone from another direction;
si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.	Soon the urine will come, then press your hand on what is obstructed by the stone that is inside the penis.
Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides;	It is broken immediately, and the stone comes out with the urine, and the patient is cured;
et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie I fil desoz la piere et I autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les II liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie;	and if you cannot do this for some reason that prevents it, tie a thread below the stone and another above it, then cut the penis directly over the stone between the two threads, then extract the stone out, and untie the thread, and clean the clotted blood that is in the wound;
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat it until it is healed.
de la piere des femmes	of the female stone
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por III choses:	It rarely happens that a stone forms in women, but if it does occur once, the treatment is difficult and is prevented for three reasons:
l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge;	One is that by chance the woman is a virgin;
et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	and the second is that one cannot find a woman who knows herself well enough to expose herself to men, especially when she is chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains;	And the third manner is that by chance one cannot find a woman who knows well in this art of midwifery;
et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil;	and the fourth manner is that the stone in the woman's body is harder and deeper than the man's stone, so it requires a deeper incision, and there is great fear involved. And if necessity demands this, then you must find an experienced midwife, but one such as this is hard to come by, and if you cannot find one, seek a discreet and chaste midwife;
et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere;	and present a wise woman in the life of women, or a woman who knows part of the art, and command her to do what you command regarding the inquiry into the stone;
et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge:	and carefully observe whether the woman is a virgin:
adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere;	then she must insert her finger into the fundament and search for the stone;
et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	and if she finds it, she should press the stone down with her finger, and recommend that she inserts her finger into the patient's vagina, and searches and presses her left hand firmly on the bladder.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse;	If she finds it, she must gently move the stone from the entrance of the bladder down to below, until it reaches the root of the thigh;
puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie;	Then cut around the stone at the root of the thigh opposite the middle of the groin, where it is moved, and feel for the stone in that area;
et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite;	and do not move his hand above the stone or below it, and let the incision be small at first;
puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont:	then insert the probe into the incision, if you feel the stone enlarge the wound as much as the stone can come out, and know that there are many kinds of stones:
c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.	that is to say, small and large and rough and smooth, long and round, and those with edges.
si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	and know the signs to understand the outcome.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	And if the blood flows, then place vitriol powder at the site, and hold it for an hour until the bleeding stops;
puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre;	Then return to your work until the stone is out, and have the instruments that I told you about for extracting stones from people to help in your work;
et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide;	and if the blood thins and it is from the artery that has been cut, then apply powder to the area and bandage with cloths and linen, and do not attempt this again, and leave the stone unextracted, for the patient may die by chance;
puis cure la plaie.	Then treat the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the heat of the blood is calmed, and the swelling subsides, then return to your work, until the stone has been expelled.
de hernie carnouse	of flesh hernia
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef;	Ramus aqueous is nothing other than a collection of moisture or white matter, which comes from the kidneys and is contained in the egg;
et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit I autre oef;	And it is called "syfac", and sometimes it is properly on the skin of the eye, so one thinks that it is another eye;
et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit;	and it is the skin of the pupil between the white syfac that we mentioned;
et ceu n’avient se poc non.	and this does not happen unless there is pus.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the generation of this aqueous retention is due to weakness that affects the testicles, and the matter spreads there.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors:	And sometimes it comes from striking the pupils, and this moisture has many colors:
ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus;	where it is a color declining to yellow, or without redness, or black, or clear white, and this happens more frequently;
et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, I poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	and these are the signs to recognize this condition, for if it is in the white syfac that we mentioned, then the abscesses are round, the pus long like the figure of an eye, and does not affect the pupil, because there is moisture all around it.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef;	And if there is moisture in the proper tissue, then the abscess appears with part of the eye, and because of this, people think it is another eye;
et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien;	and if the moisture is between the skin of the testicles and the white membrane, then one can feel it well;
donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	then when you wish to know the color of the moisture, test it thoroughly in all directions, as the form has been described above.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	According to what comes after the intromissory part, judge what is within.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors;	And when we treat it with iron, the patient must be bathed according to his strength and the fullness of his body;
puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz;	then lay him on his back on something slightly elevated, and place many cloths under him;
puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des II costelz dou keur des coions;	Then sit on his left side, and instruct the attendant to sit on the right, and extend the rod to one of the two ribs below the heart.
puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir;	Then take the scalpel and cut through the skin between the testicles down to near the root, and make your incision perfectly straight until you reach the white fat layer, and peel it back gently as much as possible;
puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a I large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont;	Then puncture the fluid-filled area with a wide incision, and drain all the fluid, and then use your forceps to stretch the opening upwards;
et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement;	and do not touch the heart of the testicles, but only the fluid-filled area;
cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue;	Cut through all or piece by piece carefully considering him subtly, for if you do not cut wisely, the fever will return.
et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac;	And if the eye jumps during your work, then reset it to its place once you have completed the task of suturing.
puis assemble les II leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then sew the two halves of the torn foreskin together at one seam, then treat it as other wounds until it is healed.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc;	And if you find the eye corrupted by another illness, then it is necessary to ligature the vessels that are suspensory, fearing the loss of blood.
puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	Then cut the foreskin along the suspensory part, and extract the eye, and treat it as we have said.
Et se aigue est assemblee en II parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont II ramices;	And if heat is gathered in two parts together, know that these are two branches;
si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset;	if you cut the other part as you did the first equally, then wipe away the blood, and put wool soaked in rose oil into the wound;
et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les II coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	and place another piece of wool soaked in wine and oil, and put over the two wounds, and cover with doubled cloths, and bind it securely according to this form:
Puis pren II drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil;	Then take two cloths, and wrap them with linen strips according to this appearance and join them by sewing at the groin of the trousers, one from the thigh up to the buttocks, and the other to the side part;
et li autre dui chief sus les II angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier;	and place the two heads on the two rings, and let all the ligature be secured in the loop of the bracelet;
et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes I cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers;	and sometimes this condition is treated with a cautery instead of iron, and you should take a fine knife-shaped cautery, cut the skin between the toes, and heat it as we have said, so that the white substance containing the fluid is exposed;
si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	take the cautery in this shape, and pierce that fluid with hooks, and scrape it with this fine hot cautery:
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout;	And cut in all the ways you can, until you remove everything;
et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef;	and be careful that the fire does not touch the eye;
et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve;	and know that this work is more safe;
et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille;	and move them to prevent bleeding, and proceed with the work of cutting;
et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	and if anything goes against you, such as an abscess or bleeding or another thing, then treat what is contrary to you according to what was said before.
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai, si fai seoir le malaide sus I siege leveit;	And if the patient is fearful and does not wish to endure this work because of its horror, then administer perforation as I tell you, and it is that when you are certain by the signs we have said that aqueous pus is there, make the patient sit on a raised seat;
pues perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors;	then pierce the abscess on the inner part across the entire span of the body, and place the puncture along the length of the body;
et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer;	and let the aperture be wide so that all the fluid can flow out;
puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee;	then place cotton on the site, and bind it, and leave it so that the remaining fluid can drain, then treat it until the wound is healed;
et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant;	and if the white cloth does not allow the fluid to exit at the wound site, then you should insert a quill or instrument used for treating the fluid in hydrops, as described above;
et eslarge I poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés VI mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	and enlarge the pocket of the wound, and check that the fluid returns, and it will clot after six months or thereabouts, and when it has clotted as before, then the patient will spend their days in this state.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the abscess of the testicles
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse;	Know that during the cutting of this vein, fear occurs in many conditions, so it seems to me that it is better to leave it as it is;
et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	and I will tell you the work and similarities of the abscess.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions;	I say then that many abscesses occur in the body, especially in the groin;
et c’est par mout de cas.	and this happens for many reasons.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion;	This is due to excessive acidity and coldness spread in the groin, or from impact;
et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors;	and the color of the abscess is according to the color of the skin;
et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief;	and finds no pain, and there is a severe abscess;
et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	and by chance, some severe abscesses are frightful and stony, and of a dusky color, and sometimes they come from the body's arteries, or swelling of veins.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois;	When it is from the arteries, it is known by the hot disposition of the abscess, when you press it with your fingers;
et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	and it is not proper for you to touch it.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois, et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars;	One who is afflicted by the swelling of veins is known by its disposition through the feeling of finger pressure, and one can properly assess the condition based on this sensation, as well as on other parts of the body;
et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	And it is that you cut the cord of the testicles, then place the egg above, and draw it out from the white membrane, and release the suspensory ligament from all parts of the egg.
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope;	If the testicle is already hardened with these new membranes, then it is necessary that you draw out the testicle, and cut it.
et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	And if it is swollen in the membrane, or inside the vessels, then it is necessary that you release all of this area, and cut it completely.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	And if the birth of the flesh is at the back, then you must cut it all away, and extract the eye, as we have said.
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when your work is completed, apply the wound with wet wool in rose oil and wine, then treat it further as needed until it heals.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the abscess of the testicles
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a I borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions, et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait;	This is an abscess wrapped in a covering similar to leather, with the softening of the testicles, and the patient moves very painfully when he goes.
et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant, et toutevoie nos vos dirons l’ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.	And the treatment for this illness is also as dangerous as the one before, and nevertheless we will tell you about it, according to what the ancients did.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois, a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment;	It is necessary that you seat the patient on a raised chair, then place the suspensory from below to your hands, covering all the vessels close to the penis, and grasp them firmly, and stretch them forcefully;
puis cope au spatumile trenchant large dou traver endroit les vasselz, tant qu’il soient descovert, et puis escorche de chescune part, si com nos avons dit en l’estraction des arteres qui sont en temples;	then cut through the large oblong spatula with a sharp edge across the vessels until they are exposed, and then skin each side, as we have said in the extraction of arteries that are in the temples;
puis i fiche une aguille ou il ait I fil double, et le lie au premier leu ou li vis est venue, et le lie derechief a l’autre chief;	then insert a needle with doubled thread and tie it at the first place where the vein is, and tie it again to the other end;
puis les cope em mileu droitement, selonc la longesce dou cors, et en trai les moistors corrumpues;	Then cut them directly in the middle, along the length of the body, and draw out the corrupted humors;
puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions;	Then treat the wound as you would others where you apply poultices, so that no vessel bleeds that nourishes one of the testicles;
car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz;	for by this no harm comes, and if the veins are full throughout, it is necessary to draw blood from all the veins;
si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	so that the testicle does not lose its nourishment due to the incision of veins, and they dry up and cannot be helped.
de la routure dou syfac	of the fracture of the cheekbone
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions;	The occurrence of this condition is due to the incision that comes from the suprapubic region, or the extension on the abdomen in the area of the inguinal canal, which causes the intestines to descend through that opening into one of the testicles;
et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces II manieres de mout de causes:	and this rupture is in the thigh or from extending it, and these two manners come from many causes:
ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses;	by impact, jumping, bending, lifting heavy loads, and similar things;
et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement;	and the signs when it is from extending the thigh are that they come little by little over a long period and do not happen suddenly;
et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	and the abscesses are equal up to the bottom because the thigh presses against the intestines.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	And the signs when it is from the section of the cheekbone are that they cause sudden pain at the beginning, and the abscesses appear differently, near the skin, because of the exit of the intestines and the body part moving away from the cheekbone.
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	And sometimes the intestines descend with the hernia, and are trapped inside, causing great pain for the patient, especially when they are compressed.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	And in these iron treatments there is fear, for which one must avoid them.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir;	And the method of treatment is that you instruct the patient to push the intestines back in with their hand into the wound if they can reach it;
puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes;	Then bind around his neck, and lift the thighs;
puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc;	then extend the heart above it, and shave all the skin of the genitals completely;
