puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir;	then insert hooks into the flanks according to what you need to open the wound, and make them such that the eye can easily exit;
puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars;	then peel off the skin that is away from the genital skin until the white fatty tissue is exposed on all sides;
puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac;	then insert your middle finger into the area behind the genitals, between the white fatty tissue that is under the skin of the penis, and between the second layer of fat, and separate what is behind the penis, and between the second layer of fat;
et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille;	and then move to the right hand inside the groin, and stretch the white surface up with your left hand, and lift the egg over all the surface towards the waist;
et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement;	and instruct the attendant to lift the egg up and loosen those who are tied behind the binding;
et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz;	and ask your two assistants if there is any part of the intestine wrapped around the white surface tightly, and if you find anything, push it back into the abdomen;
puis pren une aguille ou il ait I gros fil fait de X filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions;	then take a needle with a thick thread made of several strands and push it into the rear part of the surface, which is behind the skin of the groin;
aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait IIII filz;	after the waist, then cut the head of the ribs that appear from the children, until there are IV children;
puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars;	then arrange them one on top of the other in the manner of a cross, and bind it with a strong cord from two sides;
puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne;	then wrap the head of the ribs that appear from the children and bind them firmly from two sides so that none of the vessels that nourish them can enter, preventing an abscess from forming;
et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi;	and place the cord again according to the first binding long by two palms from that point, and after these two bindings leave the skin underneath the scrotum large by one palm;
et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte;	and then all around according to the curvature that the eye carries;
puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant;	then cut in the part that is away from the skin of the scrotum, until the blood flows, and the bowel, as we have said before;
puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	then apply moistened wool in oil to the wounds, and wrap them with the linen we have mentioned.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	And sometimes the white vein that we have mentioned is cauterized after the incision, out of fear of blood loss.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui;	For this happens often, and leave the bandage on until it falls off by itself;
et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;	and if it delays in falling off, soak it in warm water, and apply what we have mentioned, until it falls off;
puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	then treat the wound with another method, until it is completely healed.
de hernie carnouse	of flesh hernia
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this case, I have never seen anyone dare to treat it with iron.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	And the ancients said that it is made like thorns that are alongside the vein, in such a way that you tie the vessels, above the waist lightly towards the back;
puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient;	then cut into it and treat the abscess of whoever is operating, until the vessel discharges;
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat it as we have said, until it is healed.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus;	Sometimes rupture occurs in the groin, as we have said, and it is evident;
et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;	and no part of the intestines descends into the scrotum, and if it does descend, it is serious, and requires repair at all times;
et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;	and if it remains too long at this stage, the wound or sore will grow worse, until the intestines are affected;
et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;	and this happens due to the extension of the sore which is in the angles, as we have said, because it becomes extended, then softened and swollen and open;
et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit;	and the treatment for this is with cauterization, as we have said before;
et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere:	and sometimes it is treated with iron in this manner:
et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois;	and have the patient lie supine on their back between your hands, then probe the swollen area of the wound to a width of three digits;
et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac;	and then extract the tissue which is below the skin as follows, then take the thread and place it on the visible part of the tissue;
et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre;	and press it firmly against the belly, then stitch the two visible parts of the tissue at the top of the thread, and stitch one and the other;
puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;	then extract the head of the thread, and do not cut any tissue or stretch the egg or anything else, as I have told you in the treatment of intestinal hernia;
puis le cure par la cure des plaies.	then treat it according to the treatment of wounds.
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And when you cut the threads, bandage and treat the wound until it is healed.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	The tissue is tight, and there is no appearance in the rupture, and the cauterization is stiff in this place, and closer to healing.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	for the softening of the skin of the genitals
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir;	Many times the skin of the testicles becomes soft in some men because the tissues inside become softened, and it appears milky.
et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil;	And it is necessary when one wishes to treat it, that the patient lie down on his back, and the leather which is softened be placed upon the natural skin;
puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a III costures ou IIII fermement;	then join the two edges at one seam, and if you wish, sew the excess of the softened leather to three seams or four firmly;
puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	then cover between the seams, and treat it as other wounds until it is healed, and remove the stitches.
dou chastrement	of the discipline
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre;	Know that castration is condemned in our law, and for this reason I would prefer not to speak of it in this book;
et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres:	and it is necessary only for two reasons:
dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure;	Therefore, one is that the physician knows how to answer when asked, and knows the treatment;
et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	and the other, because we often need to castrate some animals to help us, such as goats and sheep and cats and other animals.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres:	I say then that castration is performed according to two methods:
ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	either by attraction, or by cutting.
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant;	In the method we perform by attraction, we make the animal sit in hot water until the testicles are softened and hanging.
puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	then grasp them with your hand until they retract and you no longer feel them.
Du chastrement de taille:	Of the treatment of the spine:
covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez;	You should castrate the animal, and press the skin of the testicles with your left hand, then attach the suspensory bandage, and cut around each one at once, after you have properly flayed them;
et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz;	and leave some of the fat on the surface and the fine fat that is on the vessels;
et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure;	and this method of castration is gentler than the one done by traction, because with traction some part of the testicles might remain accidentally, causing the animal to desire lust;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	then treat the wound until it is healed.
des hermofrodites	On hermaphrodites
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes:	Hermpheidry is according to two manners in men:
l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	one of which is that between the two thighs it opens as much as the figure of a woman's body would, where there is hair, and sometimes encircles the urine.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	And the other method is for women, and it should be applied to the wrist like a rod and two fingers.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies;	And the treatment of the man and the woman is that you cut the adjacent tissues all around, and treat them as other wounds;
en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	in the second manner, for men whose urine sprays out from the skin of the thighs, there is no treatment.
de la tentigene	of tension
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir;	Tentigene is a tissue attached to the genital area, so that it is too ugly to see;
et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	and some women have it as large as a hand, and this is the condition to be treated.
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement;	It is necessary to soak the excess of the tension with your hand or fingers, and then cover lightly;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	and do not go too deep, so that no blood seeps out, then treat it with another treatment until it is healed;
et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	and for another flesh that appears at the mouth of the throat, and when you touch it, it may break apart, and it resembles a quill, and because of this, the ancients called it "quill disease".
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	It is necessary that you treat it as we have said regarding tendon treatment, and care for it until it is healed.
de erratique	of erratic
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis;	It is erratic when the nature of the woman is not perceived, or the opening is small;
et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est;	and it is natural from birth, or accidental due to illness that has occurred;
ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit;	whether it is by flesh attached, or of thin or thick skin, and is made deep in the flesh, or ribs, or inside, or wherever;
et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir;	and prevent conception, and childbirth, and perhaps menstruation from occurring;
et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	and the knowledge of these things is by observation of the bile.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	If the obstruction is close and apparent, then treat it with your fingers or with a catheter.
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi:	If it is of thin skin, and it is close to the ribs, then hurry, and cut in this manner:
met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes;	place your two fingers together, and have the woman lie on her back, spreading her legs;
puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens;	then spread the two ribs apart, so that the thin skin is cut, and it is over the swelling;
puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	Then take wool, and melt it in oil, and apply it to the site, and have the woman lie on her back each day so that she cannot stand.
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	And if the sialagogue is hard and thick, then you should scrape it with a spatula resembling a myrtle leaf.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope;	If the obstruction is due to flesh, suspend it at the olecranon and cut it away;
et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef;	and have the blood-stanching medicines ready, such as vinegar, dragon's blood, incense, and egg whites;
puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder;	then apply a bandage of flax wide enough that the wound cannot close;
et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec;	and keep it open for a long time, and dress it with a tent of dry linen;
puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then proceed with other treatments until he is healthy.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	And when flesh is dead in a wound, it must be cut according to this method, except for deeply seated abscesses.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	For in the deeply seated abscess that is in the wound, one should not attempt to cut it open.
des emorroides	of hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul;	Hemorrhoids are openings of veins that without proper treatment become hard.
et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	and I have already mentioned in the section the similarities of them, and the signs, and here I will say those that are curable.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	I say that hemorrhoids and hard lumps, when they are perfectly formed in the wound, and do not appear to the touch, should not be treated with a cautery.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	Those who have the mouth of the ulcer, which can be felt, are those whom one can cure.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses;	It is necessary then that you place the woman in a cold room, then pull out the tumor with pliers, and cut it at its roots, then apply powder of medicines that constrict bleeding, such as oak bark and dragon's blood and frankincense, and similar things;
puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide;	then place her feet against the wall for an hour, then put her in cold water;
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	And if bleeding occurs, make the patient sit in a decoction of sumac and pomegranate peel and gall and similar things, and then take barley flour, and mix it with honey and oil, and make one plaster on their back.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	And if it stops bleeding, that is good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir;	If not, apply cupping to the back and breasts without injuring them;
puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	then take wool, and soak it in plantain juice or in elderberry juice with old wine, and apply to the area.
Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when the abscess subsides, treat the area with ointment until it is healed;
et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul;	and what is called "albathir" is red and resembles a sharp head, so it must be cut as I have said about the thelul;
et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then treat him until he is healthy.
des apostemes de la marris	for abscesses of the flesh
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	Many types of abscesses occur in the flesh, such as canker sores and stone abscesses and herpes and ulcers and fistulas and hemorrhoids and hot abscesses, and many other diseases that I have mentioned in the division.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe;	Therefore, it is necessary for me to discuss in this treatise the hot abscess that occurs in the thigh, which is not among those that affect the bowels;
et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	and if you wish to know the work of iron, observe whether the abscess is sharp at the beginning of its appearance, and full of heat and fever, and turns red if you can see it.
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie;	Then do not hurry to pierce it, but allow it to come to a head until the pain subsides;
et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus I siege, et ait II petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe;	and then have the patient sit on a chair, and place two small stools for him to lean against, support his back, and position his legs so that they are bent at the knee;
et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien;	and let his thighs be spread apart, and place his arms under his knees, and bind them well with a good rope;
puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme;	then place the patient on his right side and bring the instrument used to work inside the mouth of the wound, which is described below;
et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide;	and it is necessary that when you bring this instrument near, you insert the tip first to determine the depth of the wound so that what enters does not go too deep and does not injure the patient;
et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve;	and if the instrument is larger, it is necessary to cover the depth of the wound with cloths so that the instrument does not harm it;
et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.	And it is necessary for him to place the tip of the instrument above, and to hold the instrument.
Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit;	And when the abscess is apparent, and it is incised by hand gently, then it must be opened at the top, at the spatumile site;
et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec;	and when the boil is emptied, it is necessary to place in the wound moistened cloths in rose oil, or in green oil;
et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites;	and place the cloth outside the wound in the middle of the dressing, and place on the outside over the dressing and over the joint clean cloths moistened with water or in which mallows have been boiled;
puis le cure aprés II jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then treat after two days of ointment application as needed, until it is healed;
et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites;	And sometimes one raises the swelling and the wound with a enema of water and honey, and then with water in which long roots of lilies and artemisia have been boiled;
puis reveigne a l’oignement.	then return to applying ointment.
Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	And if the wound is laid open in the morsel, then you must avoid treating it with iron, but treat it as we have said in the section.
de l’enfantement	Of childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar:	It is necessary first for the midwife to know the appearance of natural childbirth, and the signs are when you see the woman strain downward, and desire to smell the air:
adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir;	then the child hastens to come out;
adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui;	then you know that this childbirth is according to the natural form, and the exit is under its head, and the afterbirth with it;
et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost;	And when you see these signs, gently press his abdomen so that the baby comes out quickly;
car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification;	for when it descends with its head, the afterbirth comes out with it, and is purified of its excesses through proper care;
et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	and those who come in another manner do not come naturally.
Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises;	For it sometimes comes upside down, with its feet first, and may come out in an abnormal position through the thighs or hands, or emerge from the abdomen or buttocks, and turn around by chance on its neck, or in other bad positions;
si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	it is necessary for the midwife to be wise and subtle in these matters, wary of error and deception, and I will show you all the positions how one should assist them.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent;	If the child comes out naturally over its head, and the woman gives birth heavily, and her strength is weak, then have her sit on a stool, or where women hold her;
et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	and prepare her nature with oil or fenugreek boiled, and then place between her two thighs the small spatula whose form is here:
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers;	and cut the membrane, and trim it to its nail so that the moisture inside flows out;
et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament;	and press the woman's abdomen until the child descends, and if it does not descend, then it is necessary to give her an enema of fenugreek mucilage with sesame oil;
puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre:	then have her take and sneeze from conditi, and hold her mouth and nose for an hour:
si istra maintenant l’enfes.	Now remove the child.
Et se les II mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc;	And if both hands come out of joint, you should reset them gently bit by bit;
et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus I siege, et li lieve les piés en haut;	and if they cannot be reset, place the patient on a chair and lift their feet up;
puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement;	then raise the chair off the ground, and support the patient so she does not fall when standing;
et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	and if the hand cannot be reset and the child dies, cut the hands with a knife that is placed here beforehand, and extract the child, then reset it properly.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés	of delivering the child onto its feet
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	When the child stands up, it is necessary to lift them up high;
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	and then turn it little by little, until it is even;
puis preigne I des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	then take one of the feet and extend it little by little.
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	When it jumps to the thighs, instruct them to grasp it, and make it sneeze from this position.
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	and may it jump out if God wills it.
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	And if it does not go further as we have said, then turn it little by little until it is according to its natural position.
Car adonques ist il legierement.	For then it moves easily.
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons, dit si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en I mortier;	And if it does not come out as we wish, take mastic from the altars, and sesame oil, and melted gum, and pound all in one mortar;
et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement, puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	and place the preparation inside and apply this ointment, then have her sit in warm water up to below the ribs;
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai I coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	and when it is softened, apply the collar of myrrh to it, and leave it for an hour;
puis la fai seoir sus I siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	then have her sit on the chair, then make her sneeze and hold her mouth and nose, and gently press her abdomen, for the child now jumps.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	of the birth of the child upon its knees
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	When the fetus comes in this form, place your hands on its head little by little;
puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor I lit;	then let her be seated on her neck, and hang her feet down, and lie her down on the bed;
et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval;	and fold her hands little by little, and then press her hands on her abdomen, and remove the cushions from under her until she is prepared to go down;
et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;	and if the child does not jump, then take his feet and move them apart, then push up his belly, then put your hands under.
et ewe l’enfant poc et poc;	and lift the child little by little;
et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	and instruct the woman to hold on as tightly as possible when the child emerges.
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	of the birth of the child who emerges with one hand hanging down
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	It is necessary for the surgeon to return the hand:
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	if it cannot be returned, then help the woman stand and walk;
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus I lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	if she cannot walk, then have her lie down on the bed and spread her legs apart;
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	then massage as I have described;
et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus I siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	and if she does not give birth, make her sit on a chair, then study to return the hand;
et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	and place the child according to its natural position, and make her sneeze, and command her to grasp as the baby comes out.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	from the exit of the child onto her neck, and let her spread out her hands, and her face turned towards her mother's back
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	It is necessary that the dislocated joint hold their hand, then turn it little by little, and move it gently;
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	and when it is even, put on the natural muscle movement of height and oil, as we have said, then command her to move little by little;
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus I siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne;	and when you have done this, make her sit on the chair, and command her to grasp;
et la fai esternuer.	And make them sneeze.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	In the same manner for the entire second part
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	When the swelling reaches this point on the entire second joint, cut into the second joint to your nail, until the moisture is emptied;
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	and if the child can move up its face and neck, cut from the mouth so that it is not held back, and move the child;
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	then push the child inside until it is positioned as needed, and instruct the woman to hold onto something;
adonques si istra legierement.	then extract gently.
de l’issue des gemelz	on the outcome of twins
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII;	Know that children often come in pairs, and sometimes three or four are born;
et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	and this is not a strange thing, and often happens.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	These are strange things, and do not live, if they ever occur;
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	I know that they are multiplied and are separated by the upper part that divides them, which is attached to the cheek;
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	and sometimes they come out as naturally as any other part, as we have said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	And if they come out forcefully, treat them as we have said, and let the hand be subtle, and do quickly and gently what needs to be done;
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	and do so as it is needed for salvation.
de plusors enfans	of many children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	Sometimes they are formed in the marrow I or II or III or IV or V or VI or VII, or even up to XV, and they are all shaped like children by the measurement of the wise sage, and it is necessary that the bailiff seize everything, for perhaps a similar thing befalls them;
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	do as is appropriate according to them.
de l’enfant mort	of the dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When you treat the woman of the dead child in the womb, as I said in the division, and it does not come out, and you are constrained to work with your hands;
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	you must know if the woman is in good health and has no accidents that would cause her fear of death;
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	It is necessary that the woman lie on her back, and let her shoulders be inclined downward, and raise her legs;
et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	and the attendant should divide her into two parts, laying her on the bed in such a way that she is not positioned for the descent of the child;
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	then rub the mouth with warm oil mixed with a decoction of horehound and fenugreek seeds, and also smear her hands with these oils and decoctions;
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere I leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	then gently press on the woman's abdomen, then find the appropriate spot where pressing is effective, and watch to see if the child is prepared to descend headfirst;
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	Place the cautery iron in his eyes or neck or mouth or palate or behind the beard or in the throat or near the sides, and if the descent is on the feet, place it on the toes and at the middle ribs;
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	and it is necessary that he hold the cautery iron in his right hand, and place the curved part between the two fingers of his left hand, and press it gently with his whole hand, and apply the iron to one of the places we have mentioned until it reaches the empty space;
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	and this is the form of the cautery iron:
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	then apply another cautery iron opposite the first one, or a third if needed, so that the extractions are equal;
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	and then stretch it evenly by moving from side to side, so that the bones can exit, and let the edges of the bone be toothed to hold the bones in place, as shown here is the form:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	And if one part remains, anoint the side with some of his oils, and press it into that part, and pull the other part;
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	and if any part remains, place this bone higher up, and do so until it all comes out.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	And if one hand comes before the other, and he cannot bring it back for grasping, then you must wrap around the finger, until it all comes out;
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	Then place it at the joint of the sole or heel, and thus you should do with the other hand, and for both feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	And if the head of an infant is large and it is tight in the birth canal, or there is a swollen assembly on the head, then you should insert two fingers between them, cut the head open, and extract the fluid;
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	where you should round it with the instrument called "almidach," of which the form comes with the instruments in the chapter that follows this one;
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	and do the same if the child has a large head naturally;
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	and then pull the bones with pliers, and if the head jumps forward and it is tight against the forceps, cut them until the moisture that is in the foot's exit is reached;
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	and if it cannot come out, cut it piece by piece until you can.
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	and if it is swollen in the belly or between the ribs, you must pierce it until the moisture flows out.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the child is on his feet, then the traction is light, and the adjustment to the mouth of the socket is light.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if it is tight in the belly or breast, you must stretch it with a drapery wrapped around your hand;
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	and cut into the belly or breast until the moisture that is inside flows out;
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	and if the other limb is removed and the head remains, push your hand in through a hole at the base, and draw it out to the mouth of the socket;
puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;	Then insert the needle at one or two places, and draw it through.
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	and if the mouth of the sore is constricted due to a hot abscess that has come upon it, one should not work on it, but rather administer moist and greasy substances;
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	and the treatment includes plasters, and applies aqueous solutions that soften and moisten.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the child is on its side, and you can make it lie flat, then treat it as we have said for a living child;
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	and if one has no power to do so, then draw the needle through in sections, and leave nothing of the second skin.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, apply the treatment we have described for large abscesses that occur in the flesh;
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	and if bleeding occurs, apply cold compresses, and use other treatments as necessary.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut I autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman in whom the fetus in her womb had died, and when another was conceived after that one, it too was stillborn.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time, abscesses came to her mouth, and it swelled so much that it burst, and began to pus heavily.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called to treat it, and I thought for a long time, and could not heal the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I applied an emplastrum of strong attraction, and out came one bone, and after several days another.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I marveled greatly, because there were no bones in the abdomen.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	I thought that they were the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	I treated the wound, and laid bare the bones, until the woman was in better condition;
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	and I tended to the woman for a long time in this way, and she would occasionally discharge a little pus from the area;
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	and I have recorded this chapter only because when masters encounter something unusual, they should know how to provide assistance.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	To return the joint to its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;	Here follows the form of the compress, which is used in the books;
et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	And to two turns at the two shoulders of the two ligaments.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	Nevertheless, the horns should be more subtle than the retort, and should be made of ebony or boxwood;
et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	and the mouth of the tube should be two fingers wide, and the edge of the wood should be one finger, and its length half a palm;
et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	and between the two ligaments should be two joints of the same tube, which are firmly fixed in each, half a palm long or a bit more;
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	and these two joints are placed at the mouth of the tube to open when the two horns are turned.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, more subtle and lighter, should be made of ebony wood or boxwood, according to the appearance of the pincers;
et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;	and have two heads with two joints, as you see, one palm in length, and two fingers wide;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	and when you wish to open the rectum with the instrument, make the woman sit on a bed, her feet hanging down and legs spread, then insert the two joints of the instrument together into the rectum, and hold the head of the instrument between her thighs;
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	then work your hand on the instrument as you did with the pincers equally, according to the amount you wish to open the rectum's opening, until it stretches as much as she desires.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;	These instruments are all mounted, and their kinds are multiplied;
et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	and when the physician has them prepared, the work is done more quickly, and they appear greater to people because of their size.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	Do not despise the instrument just because you have not prepared it, for their need is not excusable.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the afterbirth is retained during childbirth, you must instruct the patient to hold her breath, and then make her sneeze by administering something suitable, and hold your hands over her mouth and nose;
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	and if she expels it because of this, so much the better.
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If not, take a poultice and make a hole in the cover, and place herbs that can open the mouth of the womb, such as chamomile, rue, anise, daisy, savory, and centaury;
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;	All these herbs, or some of them, should be boiled in water over the fire;
puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;	then place a tube in the opening of the pot and the other end in the mouth of the mare, and let it flow until the vapor comes inside the mare;
puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	then make her sneeze, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	The second joint jumps quickly.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;	And if she remains after this treatment and does not improve, instruct the patient to moisten her left hand in oil of sesame or in mastic of hellebore, and then place it on the affected area, and seek a second opinion;
et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	and when she has found it, take it and stretch it little by little straightly, so that the fetus does not fall during extraction;
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;	but it is necessary to move it gently to the right and to the left, and then straighten;
si venra et se desaerdra.	it will come and dislocate again.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the opening of the nostril is narrow, we have described the treatment of sneezing and the fumigation of herbs;
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	and if it does not respond to all that we have said, be careful not to force it;
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	but it is necessary to tie the affected area of the nostril to the woman's thigh, then administer an enema of tetrachordal ointment;
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;	it will soften and return, and come out on its own;
mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	however, when it happens, a bad smell comes to the stomach and head, and troubles the patient.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu:	Therefore, appropriate fumigations should be given to them:
aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	some of the ancients have tried fumigation with cabbage and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The form of the instrument with which one fumigates the woman to retain her flowers and secondine is as follows:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And it is like glass in appearance, and one places the head subtly in the nature, and the cheeks wide over the fire;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	and let the fumigation be over the charcoal, and continue it until it is spent, and then start another one.
de percier lou fondement	to pierce the fundament
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born who do not have the anus developed, instead it is closed by fine membranes:
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	Therefore, it is necessary for the surgeon to pierce that spot properly with its appropriate tool, and not with a sharp spatula, and be careful so as not to touch it.
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then apply wet flax in wine and oil, then continue treating with ointment until he is healed.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that it will stay in place, insert a wire through the hole, and leave it there for several days, and remove it when the child wants to go to rooms.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme;	And sometimes these obstructions come from the sudden closure of a wound or abscess;
si covient coper celui soudement:	it is necessary to cut open that sudden closure:
si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	and treat it as we have said about the sinew of flesh.
de la fistule dou fondement	of the fistula of the anus
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;	Fistulas that come from below the fundament are nodular, and those that come near the fundament or in the space between the two parts may be one fistula or multiple;
et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans;	And when that knotting is old, it works, and still moisture attends white or subtle poultice, and sometimes these fistulas are perforating;
et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	And they are known by what comes out in diarrhea or flatulence when the patient has diarrhea, and sometimes worms come out.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge;	And there are fistulas that penetrate up to the bladder, and up to half of the penis;
et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	and reach up to the joint of the thigh, and up to the root of the knee.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one knows the perforating fistula at the anus, and not perforating:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	And it is that you place your thumb at the base, and insert a fine needle of brass or iron into the fistula when there is no curvature.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if there is curvature, then insert a fine thread of linen or horsehair until you feel the thread or hair with your thumb;
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	and if you do not feel it, and there is no passage for discharge or gas or truth, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie;	you know that it does not penetrate;
si te haste dou curer.	then hurry to treat it.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula reaches to the bladder or to the urethra, then it causes urination, and cannot be stopped by medicine.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it reaches the joint of the thigh, then the thread comes to that place;
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	If there is no curvature and the cause of the pain around it is not apparent, then it will become a bow (a permanent deformity), and medication or soothing ointment will be ineffective.
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	And in these persistent fistulas, there is no cure other than diligent work, and the vanity of foolish doctors who meddle with them.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos;	In the case that is not persistent and is not old, there is hope for healing by iron, as I have experienced, and it is when the patient lies down on their back with their spine between your hands;
et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	and lift the patient's legs up to their thighs, and have the thighs inclined towards the abdomen;
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	then insert a tent of linen, or one made of cloth if there is curvature, until you know where the tent reaches.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet;	If the patient feels it around the fundament, then you must insert your finger there; if then you feel that the tent has been pierced,
et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	and it is uncovered where you feel between your finger the surface or flesh, then you know that it is perforated;
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	do not treat it further as it cannot be healed.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	It is said that some can be well treated, but this happens rarely;
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	and the treatment that is done involves heating the cautery gently according to the width of the fistula, as was said before;
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement;	and insert it completely hot into the fistula until it reaches near the fundament;
et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	and do this two or three times until you know that the charred parts are burned away, which resemble a feather of a bird;
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	and then treat it with moistened bandages soaked in butter until the flesh grows back, and then treat it with an ointment that promotes tissue growth and healing.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	If he is thus healthy, it is well.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If this cannot be healed by any other means;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	and if the pus enters and does not reach the root which is at the base, and there is a thick layer of flesh or tissue between your bone and the abscess, and you see the fistula under this covering of the chest;
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	cut it from the beginning of the fistula and then cut towards the abscess, and apply the cautery afterward until you reach the head of the abscess;
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;	and the tent will be delivered, and it will fall;
puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	then cleanse those damaged tissues that resemble a bird's feather, and leave none behind.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the flesh resists and does not allow you to reach the work, then cauterize it with fire or a dry medication.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses:	For the fire cautery combines two good things:
c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	that is to say, the removal of adherent tissues, and stopping the blood and drying the moisture;
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	then treat moist tents with butter or ground substances until the place secretes pus, and remove the burnt tissues in the pus;
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	then treat the wound with hot applications and penetrating medicines that harden the tissue, and the medicines will dry.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is restored, it is healed and does not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if a fistula comes up from the deepest part of the fundament, and is distant from the body, touch that place with your finger and inquire about it.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre II est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des III manieres:	If you feel the tent, and there are two layers of cloth or skin where it is close to piercing, there must be no fear but faith and hope, through the administration of one of the three methods:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	or you cauterize it as we have said, or you cut it down to the base, or if you can place tents and treat it as in the first case;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	and do not go too deep, so that you do not cut the tissue that holds the base, and vomiting occurs unwillingly;
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	then treat it as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	by chance it will be healed, or you remove that covering and clean it since it has been cut near the base, either by tenting or with another appropriate instrument;
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	Then cleanse the wounded flesh that is in the wound as much as you can.
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement:	Then strive to restore the wound and to heal the fistula in the part away from the fundament:
si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	it will be easier for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere:	And sometimes fistulas occur in this manner:
et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	and it is when you insert the probe into the fistula, and it is in the crease near the fundament under the skin, then take a probe with this shape at the tip:
Et i boute I fil tort en II, et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And insert the thread in a twisted manner into position two, and insert the probe along the entire length of the thread into the fistula until it reaches the tip.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it is perforated in the margin of the fundament internally, then extract the thread from that passage, such that you insert your finger into the fundament;
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les II chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse I jor ou II;	and pull the head of the thread, and bring the two shoulders together, and hold them to each other, and leave it for one day or two;
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	and restrain it several times until the thread cuts through the tissue between them, and they separate;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	then treat the wound until it is sealed and healed.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not open, pierce it in all ways that you can, if it is not too hard.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it is not proper to operate on it if it is too hard, and then treat it, as we have said, until it is healed.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The form of the spinous process where one makes the fistula is very sharp on one side and cutting;
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	and on the other side it is not, so that one does not cut what should not be cut, as you see here:
des emorroydes	for hemorrhoids
Emorrydes sont selonc II manieres:	Emorrhoids occur in two manners:
ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement;	where they are inside the fundament, like grains of sand, and there are small and large ones, and in the course blood is present, and there may be one or more, and they are deviated from the fundament and at the head of the fundament;
mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	but those that are deviated have little moisture, and still contain a small amount of yellow water or a small amount of blood, and they have the color of flesh;
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	and the treatment for those who have them inside the fundament is that you instruct the patient to abstain from going out of bed until the fundament heals, and this applies to children;
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	hurry and grasp it with forceps, where you hold it with your nail, then cut it off at its root;
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a I drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	and if the hooks cannot hold them due to moisture, they take them with one finger, or with cotton, or with a piece of cloth;
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	and extract them with your two hands, then cut them, and apply some warm powders that are used for cauterization;
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, pues les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	or you cauterize them as it is said in the chapter on cauterization, then treat them with other treatments until they are healed;
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	and if the hemorrhoid cannot be removed, administer a harsh and sharp enema to the patient to cleanse what is in the anus so that it can exit freely;
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	when the patient is constipated, and if the filaments are hard in the anus, then the treatment is light;
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	And it is that you grasp them with your nail or pincers, and cut them, then treat them as we have said, until they are healed, and that they fear the incision by iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere:	It is necessary that you manage the suturing according to this manner:
pren I fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les II chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille, et si soit dou large;	take the thread and twist it onto a needle, then pull the thread from above and pierce the needle from another side, and turn the two ends of the thread under the needle, and let it be wide;
et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse I por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	and tightly pull the thread, then tie it off, and remove the needle, and do this for all of them, leaving one to allow the excess blood to flow out;
puis met sus le fondement I drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	Then place a moistened piece of cloth in rose oil or cerate on the foundation, and place it there, and instruct the patient to rest;
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then leave them until they fall off, and when they have fallen off, treat them with ointment and other treatments until they are healed.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	from the dryness of the bowels or foundation
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Often there is constipation of feces in the intestines, and by the constraint of nature, and when the illness is old and medicine is of no use.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	It is necessary that you cut with the tip of a spatula or your nail through the skin above, without leaving it to become moist.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	then treat it until it is dry as necessary;
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	and if it does not dry, then shave more forcefully than before until it heals significantly, and let it be scarred;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat him until he is healthy.
dou fremit	with trembling
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	The flea is a small striped appearance on the body, and moves very quickly;
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	and sometimes it is found in the cold, and one feels it as if frozen with shivering, and it spreads throughout the body, and more so in the hands than anywhere else.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the treatment is that you take a quill from a goose feather or a strong bird feather, and place the quill on the shiver, until the circles surround the shiver completely;
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	then turn your hand around the quill until you cover all around the shiver, and move it quickly, and shake the shiver from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you wish, do this with a tube of linen or iron according to this form, and let it be fine underneath and threaded above:
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser.	Do not pierce, to keep the hair from moving, and press the hairs.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	And if you wish, cauterize the tremor as it is described before in the chapter on cauterization.
de la forme dou clistere	of the form of the enema
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet;	Sometimes a enema is made of silver or sorrel, or molten wool or bran;
et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	and sometimes these instruments small and large are used, according to the needs of those to whom they are administered.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Those who are treated in the care of children and those who are weak and in pain are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The form of the enema, small and large, is as follows, or the belly is bound in this manner:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez;	and there should be a separation where the abdomen is bound as you see, and the rectum inside is perforated;
et ait a l’un des costez II pertus, et en l’autre I;	and on one side there should be two holes, and on the other side one;
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus, et ait entre chescun pertus I doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus I fil fort de fil crut tort en X ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	And let the pouch where medicines are placed be made from a bladder of an animal or parchment, and let it be pierced all around with small holes, and have one finger’s width between each hole, then insert a strong cord of rawhide thread in ten or so around, and join the pouch as if it were a drum.
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize;	And when the medicine is inside, tie it to the instrument with a strong thread, then administer as an enema;
et c’est li forme dou cercle:	and this is the form of the circle:
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	And let the medicine not be too hot nor too cold, and anoint the tip of the enema with oil or egg yolk, or similar substance, then insert it gently;
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses II mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit, et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet;	Then the minister presses both hands together onto him until he is fully turned, then removes the enema, and lifts the patient's legs against the wall, and if the medicine needs to come out, let it drain as much as possible;
et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	and if he sleeps one full night, then there is greater help.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you administer an enema in a case of diarrhea and the medicine wants to come out quickly, then repeat it until he is well.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por I enfant;	And if the hemorrhoids are at the fundament, or an abscess, then the enema should be as fine as for a child;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	and this is the form of the fine enema in which the skin is stretched:
des plaies	of wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies;	We have already said in the section about the treatment of wounds;
or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	We will tell you about the treatments of hands and medicine, according to their fulfillment.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are diverse according to how they are made, and according to the places where the wounds are made, and what they are made of.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The things by which wounds are made are from falling stones, and the cutting of swords and knives, or lances or staffs or arrows, or similar things;
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	or they are made according to the parts of the body, such as a wound that falls on the neck, or on the head, or the foot, or the belly, or the liver, and similar members;
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	and I will tell you the treatment for each wound, and I will begin with simple head wounds, because the memory will come in its chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans, et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut:	I say that when a simple wound comes to the head and the bone is not broken, be careful if it is from falling stones or similar things, and the skin is completely torn and the wound is large, and you fear the rising of a hot abscess:
