et plus dedens c’aillors, et poc desalue devant et derrier.	and more inward than otherwise, and slightly dislocated in front and behind.
Et li conoissance de sa dislocations dedens si est que quant on joint la jambe malaide avec la sainne, si est plus longe, et apert plus li malaides genous que li sains, et ne puet li malaides doubler son genoil au feu;	And the recognition of an inward dislocation is that when joining the affected leg with the healthy one, it appears longer, and the patient's knee appears more bent than the healthy one, and the patient cannot bend their knee towards the fire;
et est li leus qui est delez enflez d’aposteme chaut, por ceu que li chiés de la cuixe vient lai.	And the area which is near the swelling of the abscess is hot, because the knee comes there.
Et li signe de celui cui il vient au defuer, si est que cist accident sont contraire a ces devant.	And the signs of him who is coming to faint are contrary to those mentioned before.
Et li signes de celui cui avient au devant, si est qu’il estent bien sa jambe selonc l’acomplissement;	And the signs of one who is affected in front are that they stretch their leg according to the completion;
toutevoie, ne double mie le genoil sens dolor, et s’on le vuet faire aler, si ne puet avant, et retient son urine, et enfle li angre, et quant il vait, si passe sus le talon.	nevertheless, they do not double their knee despite pain, and if one wants to make them go forward, they cannot advance, and they hold back their urine, and the groin swells, and when they walk, they step over the heel.
Et li signes de celui cui il avient derrier, si est qu’il ne puet espandre son genoil, ne doubler, et est celle jambe plus torte de l’autre, et li angre est mollifié, et est li chiés de la cuixe au leu desoz les costes.	And the signs of him who is coming to a condition behind are that he cannot extend his knee or bend it, and that leg is more crooked than the other, and the ankle is softened, and the head of the thigh is in a position below the ribs.
Li ramenemens de ceste semblance de dislocation si est que tu rewarde se li dislocations est anciainne, et elle demore selonc sa disposition, si n’i a nule cure;	The treatment for this type of dislocation is that you observe whether the dislocation is old, and it remains according to its condition, with no specific care;
et n’i covient mie qu’il ait presumption.	and it is not appropriate for them to have confidence.
Et en celi dont li dislocation est fresche, et c’est des IIII manieres de dislocation, si te haste que tu tornes la jointe, et l’esten dedens et defuer, et la muef a destre et senestre;	And in the one where the dislocation is fresh, and it is of the four types of dislocation, hasten to return the joint, and stretch it inward and outward, and move it right and left;
par aventure si revenra, et n’a mestier d’autre cure.	and perhaps it will return, and no other treatment is needed.
Et s’il ne revient en ceste maniere, si covient que tu apareilles I ministre fort, et esten la jambe fort a II mains, ou a I liien que soit liiez sus lou genoil;	And if it does not return in this manner, then you must prepare a strong minister, and stretch the leg strongly with two hands, or with one ligature that is tied above the knee;
et uns autres ministres estende sa main desus en teil maniere qu’il boute ses mains desoz ses asseles, puis l’estrigne d’un souef liien sus la cuixe;	and another minister should stretch his hand above in such a manner that he places his hands beneath the buttocks, then bind it with a single tight ligature on the thigh;
et uns autres tigne lou chief dou liien;	and some others hold the head of the joint;
et estendent amont et aval tuit a une fois, tant que li malaide soit levez de terre a une fois, et demoure pendans.	and extend both up and down at once, so that the patient is lifted off the ground all at once, and suspend them.
Ceste maniere d’estension si est commune as IIII semblances, et se li dislocation est revenue, si com nos avons dit, c’est bien.	This method of extension is common to the four similar cases, and if the dislocation has returned, as we have said, it is well.
Se ceu non, si covient mettre cure a sa semblance.	If not, then you must apply treatment as appropriate.
Quant li dislocations est au pardedens, si covient que tu sovines le malaide sus son costeit sain, puis met le liien sus la racine de la cuixe, et le leu qui est desoz l’angre, puis estent le liien en haut devers l’angre, et devers la forcele;	When the dislocation is towards the inside, you must lift the patient onto their healthy side, then place the joint at the root of the thigh, and the area below the armpit, then extend the joint upwards toward the armpit, and toward the shoulder.
puis preigne uns autres ministres ses bras, et embraice le gros leu de la cuixe malaide, et l’estende au defuer forment:	then take other assistants to hold his arms, and embrace the thick part of the affected thigh, and extend it forcefully outward:
si revenra a son leu maintenant;	It will return to its place now;
et ceste maniere de dislocation est plus legiere des autres.	and this type of dislocation is less severe than the others.
Et se tu ne la pues serrer en ceste maniere que nos avons dit, si covient que tu lies les II piés dou malaide ensamble d’un fort liien souef sus les II talons, et sus les II genous, et soit li jambe malaide estendue II dois plus que li autres;	And if you cannot secure it in the manner we have described, then you must bind both of the patient's feet together with a strong cord just above the two heels, and also above the two knees, and let the affected leg be extended two palms longer than the other.
puis soit pendus sus le chief d’un fust, et soit en sus de terre II bras de lonc;	then suspend him from the top of a post, and let it be two arm lengths above the ground;
puis comande a I ministre qu’il embraice le chief de la cuixe, et soit uns autres ministres pendans avec le malaide, qui embraice forment la cuixe, car li jointure revient maintenant hastanment.	then instruct one minister to embrace the top of the thigh, and let another minister hang with the patient, who firmly embraces the thigh, because the joint will now quickly return.
Et quant li dislocations est au defuer, si gise li malaides, si com nos avons dit en celui qui a gilbositeit, et estraigne I liien sus la jambe malaide proprement, et sus le peis ausi;	And when the dislocation is out of place, the patient lies down, as we have said regarding him who has gout, and tightly bind the limb on the affected leg, and also on the foot.
puis met II tisons, I au chief et I autre as piez, puis fiche I tison entre les cuixes au malaide emmi la forme;	then place two torches, one at the head and one at the feet, then insert a torch between the thighs of the patient in the proper position;
et ait plantei de drapelz moistes entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide, puis estende chescuns ministre devers lui, et li mires mette igal a sa main la dislocation.	and have placed damp cloths around it so that it does not burn the patient, then each assistant extends towards him, and the physician places his hand equally on the dislocation.
S’elle revient, c’est boin.	If it returns, it is good.
Se ce non, met sus .ie. table, et le presse ensi com nos avons dit en la gilbositeit, et gise li malaides sus le sain costeit.	If not, place him on the table and press as we have said regarding gilbositeit, and let the patient lie on the healthy side.
Et quant li dislocations est devant, si covient estendre la jambe malaide hastanment, et selonc ce que j’ai dit;	And when the dislocation is in front, it is necessary to quickly extend the affected leg as I have said;
et mette li mires sa paine d’estre sus l’angre malaide, puis presse a l’autre main, et l’estent aval devers lou genoil.	And let the physician exert himself to be on the affected side, then press with the other hand, and stretch it down towards the knee.
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les II hainches;	And if the dislocation is towards the front, it is not appropriate to stretch the patient downward or lift them up, but rather they should be positioned as if the thigh were dislocated forward, as we have said about the position when lying on both thighs;
et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table;	and let the patient lie on their back, and the limb be stretched as we have said previously, and one should press above the joint onto the table;
et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz;	and it will be correct when the patient extends their legs, and they will be even;
adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve;	Then place the thighs together, apply the plaster, and wrap them tightly with a bandage so that the thigh does not move;
et se repose III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus;	and let it rest for three or four days, then remove the bandage and reapply the plaster;
et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse III jors;	and if you see that they are even, wrap them as before and leave it for three days;
puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	then remove the bandage, and have him walk gently, until the limb is healed.
de la dislocation dou genoil	Of the dislocation of the knee
Li genous est desaluez selonc III manieres:	The knee is dislocated in three ways:
c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier;	that is to say, inward and outward, and backward;
et ne desalue point devant.	and do not reset before.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez;	And the sign is that you instruct the patient to bend his leg at the thigh, and if it does not rest there, know that it is dislocated;
et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez;	and the restoration of all is that you make the patient sit upright, and extend his leg if he can, and place your back against his face, and put his foot on your feet;
puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les II costez dou genoil forment;	then take his knee in your palms, and draw it between your hands, then bend the two sides of the knee gently;
et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement;	and another minister extends his foot, so that the knee returns to its place, and the sign is that he rests his leg on the thigh lightly;
et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie;	and apply the plaster on it, and raise the leg at the thigh, and bind them together tightly for three days or four, then loosen it;
et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	and the patient does not work to walk until the limb is healed and strengthened.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	And if the limb is not properly set, apply strong extension as we have said in the treatment of the thigh, until it is healed
de la dislocation dou talon	of the dislocation of the heel
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The heels are sometimes bruised, and sometimes completely dislocated, both internally and externally.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee:	And the sign is that the ankle is swollen, and feels soft in the area where it is dislocated:
li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	the reduction is easy, and it should be gently extended with his hands when he is slightly moved.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville;	And when it is quickly reduced, you must make the patient sit upright, and have one assistant hold him a distance away by the leg, above the ankle;
puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut;	Then draw the foot towards you with your right hand, and then with your left hand twice, then place it upright, and firmly push the foot upwards;
et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet;	and do this twice, as we have said, both pushing and pulling the foot;
s’elle revient, c’est bien;	if it returns, it is well;
se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient;	if not, then restart the work, for it will return;
et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide;	and if it cannot return in this manner, then have the patient lie on their back on the ground, and firmly place a lever between their thighs in the ground, and tie ropes around them so that the patient does not move;
puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet;	Then the minister should hold the thigh, and another minister should extend the foot with his hands or on a board, and bind it at the neck of the foot;
puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent;	Then each minister should extend equally, and the patient should be firmly between the thighs of the patient when they are stretching him;
puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	Then the physician should place the dislocation in his hands equally, and another minister should hold the healthy leg behind, and the dislocation will quickly return to its proper position.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois;	And when it is properly set, apply the plaster and bandages tightly, and bind the foot to the leg, and guard the nerves that are on the back of the ankle, so that the binding is not too tight;
puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain;	then leave it for two days or three, and if the ligaments soften, then stretch it;
puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors;	then loosen it on the third day or fourth, and forbid the patient from walking for four days;
et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	and if he walks before this期限，他可能会再次脱位。 
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if an abscess comes up, you must treat it as we have said elsewhere, until it is healed.
des dois	of the two
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When both are dislocated, they must be gently extended without strain, and this is an easy task.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne;	And if the dislocation is in any notch of the back of the foot, you must have the patient sit on a flat surface or on a .ie. table straight, and place your foot against what appears of these joints, then press strongly with your foot until it returns;
et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie;	and when it is even, and nothing appears, place under the sole of the foot a board with II joints, then pull strongly, and leave it for III days, then untie it;
et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and have him rest until he is healed.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	of wound and of dislocation together
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert:	When a wound comes with the dislocation, and one wishes to restore it, many times the patient dies:
si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis;	Do not be presumptuous in the treatment if you are not wise in the art and have not used it for a long time, and if you are not compassionate and patient, nor bold;
et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit;	and begin with things that soothe an acute abscess, and leave the patient in God’s hands if you see no hope for recovery;
et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne;	and when you see hope for recovery, now reset the limb to its place so that the hot abscess may come to life;
et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis;	and when the limb is in place, administer things that soothe an acute abscess, and treat the wound as necessary with drying ointments;
et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples;	And if with the dislocation there is a fracture, and small bones displaced, remove them, and do as we have said in simple diseases;
et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	And guard against entering a path of fear as I have said, for it is your duty according to your Creator, and for the skill in your arm and your body.
